import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import {
  collection,
  getDocs,
  addDoc,
  deleteDoc,
  updateDoc,
  doc,
  query,
  orderBy,
  Timestamp,
} from 'firebase/firestore';
import { format } from 'date-fns';
import {
  Megaphone,
  Plus,
  Trash2,
  X,
  Loader2,
  Info,
  AlertTriangle,
  CheckCircle2,
  Wrench,
  ToggleLeft,
  ToggleRight,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { useAuth } from '../context/AuthContext';
import { useToast } from '../components/Toast';
import ConfirmModal from '../components/ConfirmModal';

type AnnouncementType = 'info' | 'warning' | 'success' | 'maintenance';

interface Announcement {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  message: string;
  type: AnnouncementType;
  isActive: boolean;
  targetAudience: 'all' | 'active' | 'expired';
  createdAt: any;
  createdBy: string;
  expiresAt: any | null;
}

const TYPE_META: Record<AnnouncementType, { label: string; icon: any; color: string; bg: string; border: string }> = {
  info: {
    label: 'Info',
    icon: Info,
    color: 'text-blue-300',
    bg: 'bg-blue-500/10',
    border: 'border-blue-500/30',
  },
  warning: {
    label: 'Warning',
    icon: AlertTriangle,
    color: 'text-amber-300',
    bg: 'bg-amber-500/10',
    border: 'border-amber-500/30',
  },
  success: {
    label: 'Success',
    icon: CheckCircle2,
    color: 'text-green-300',
    bg: 'bg-green-500/10',
    border: 'border-green-500/30',
  },
  maintenance: {
    label: 'Maintenance',
    icon: Wrench,
    color: 'text-orange-300',
    bg: 'bg-orange-500/10',
    border: 'border-orange-500/30',
  },
};

const AUDIENCE_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  all: 'All users',
  active: 'Active subscribers only',
  expired: 'Expired subscribers only',
};

interface CreateModalProps {
  adminEmail: string;
  onClose: () => void;
  onCreated: (a: Announcement) => void;
}

function CreateModal({ adminEmail, onClose, onCreated }: CreateModalProps) {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [message, setMessage] = useState('');
  const [type, setType] = useState<AnnouncementType>('info');
  const [audience, setAudience] = useState<'all' | 'active' | 'expired'>('all');
  const [expiresAt, setExpiresAt] = useState('');
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const { showToast } = useToast();
  const overlayRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  async function handleCreate() {
    if (!title.trim() || !message.trim()) {
      showToast('Title and message are required', 'error');
      return;
    }
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      const data = {
        title: title.trim(),
        message: message.trim(),
        type,
        isActive: true,
        targetAudience: audience,
        createdAt: Timestamp.now(),
        createdBy: adminEmail,
        expiresAt: expiresAt ? Timestamp.fromDate(new Date(expiresAt)) : null,
      };
      const ref = await addDoc(collection(db, 'announcements'), data);
      onCreated({ id: ref.id, ...data } as Announcement);
      showToast('Announcement created', 'success');
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Failed to create', 'error');
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div
      ref={overlayRef}
      className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm p-4"
      onClick={e => { if (e.target === overlayRef.current) onClose(); }}
    >
      <div className="w-full max-w-lg rounded-2xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 shadow-2xl">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-4 border-b border-slate-700">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-indigo-600">
              <Megaphone className="h-4 w-4 text-white" />
            </div>
            <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold text-white">New Announcement</h2>
          </div>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-colors">
            <X className="h-5 w-5" />
          </button>
        </div>
        <div className="p-5 space-y-4">
          {/* Type selector */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-2">Type</label>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2">
              {(Object.keys(TYPE_META) as AnnouncementType[]).map(t => {
                const meta = TYPE_META[t];
                const Icon = meta.icon;
                return (
                  <button
                    key={t}
                    onClick={() => setType(t)}
                    className={`flex flex-col items-center gap-1.5 rounded-lg border py-2.5 px-2 text-xs font-medium transition-colors ${
                      type === t
                        ? `${meta.border} ${meta.bg} ${meta.color}`
                        : 'border-slate-600 text-slate-400 hover:border-slate-500'
                    }`}
                  >
                    <Icon className="h-4 w-4" />
                    {meta.label}
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
          {/* Title */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Title</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={title}
              onChange={e => setTitle(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="e.g. Scheduled maintenance on May 10"
              maxLength={100}
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>
          {/* Message */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Message</label>
            <textarea
              value={message}
              onChange={e => setMessage(e.target.value)}
              rows={3}
              placeholder="Full announcement text shown to users…"
              maxLength={500}
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500 resize-none"
            />
            <p className="text-right text-[10px] text-slate-500 mt-0.5">{message.length}/500</p>
          </div>
          {/* Audience + Expires */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <div>
              <label className="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Target Audience</label>
              <select
                value={audience}
                onChange={e => setAudience(e.target.value as any)}
                className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
              >
                <option value="all">All Users</option>
                <option value="active">Active Only</option>
                <option value="expired">Expired Only</option>
              </select>
            </div>
            <div>
              <label className="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Expires At (optional)</label>
              <input
                type="datetime-local"
                value={expiresAt}
                onChange={e => setExpiresAt(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="flex gap-3 px-5 pb-5">
          <button onClick={onClose} className="flex-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-700 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-600 transition-colors">
            Cancel
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={handleCreate}
            disabled={saving}
            className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-50 transition-colors"
          >
            {saving ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> : <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />}
            Publish
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function AnnouncementsPage() {
  const { adminUser } = useAuth();
  const { showToast } = useToast();
  const [items, setItems] = useState<Announcement[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [showCreate, setShowCreate] = useState(false);
  const [togglingId, setTogglingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [deletingId, setDeletingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  // Confirmation state
  const [confirmToggle, setConfirmToggle] = useState<{ id: string; current: boolean } | null>(null);
  const [confirmDelete, setConfirmDelete] = useState<Announcement | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      try {
        const snap = await getDocs(
          query(collection(db, 'announcements'), orderBy('createdAt', 'desc'))
        );
        setItems(snap.docs.map(d => ({ id: d.id, ...(d.data() as Omit<Announcement, 'id'>) })));
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(err);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
    load();
  }, []);

  async function executeToggle() {
    if (!confirmToggle) return;
    const { id, current } = confirmToggle;
    setTogglingId(id);
    try {
      await updateDoc(doc(db, 'announcements', id), { isActive: !current });
      setItems(prev => prev.map(a => a.id === id ? { ...a, isActive: !current } : a));
      showToast(`Announcement ${!current ? 'activated' : 'deactivated'}`, 'success');
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Failed', 'error');
    } finally {
      setTogglingId(null);
    }
  }

  async function executeDelete() {
    if (!confirmDelete) return;
    setDeletingId(confirmDelete.id);
    try {
      await deleteDoc(doc(db, 'announcements', confirmDelete.id));
      setItems(prev => prev.filter(a => a.id !== confirmDelete.id));
      showToast('Announcement deleted', 'success');
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Failed', 'error');
    } finally {
      setDeletingId(null);
    }
  }

  function formatTs(ts: any): string {
    if (!ts) return '—';
    try { return format(ts.toDate(), 'MMM d, yyyy HH:mm'); } catch { return '—'; }
  }

  const activeCount = items.filter(a => a.isActive).length;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6 max-w-3xl">
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Announcements</h1>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">
            {activeCount} active · {items.length} total · Shown to users in-app based on audience
          </p>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => setShowCreate(true)}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 transition-colors"
        >
          <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
          New Announcement
        </button>
      </div>

      {loading ? (
        <div className="space-y-3">
          {Array.from({ length: 3 }).map((_, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="h-24 rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 animate-pulse" />
          ))}
        </div>
      ) : items.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 py-20 text-center">
          <Megaphone className="h-10 w-10 text-slate-600 mx-auto mb-3" />
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm font-medium">No announcements yet</p>
          <p className="text-slate-500 text-xs mt-1">Create one to broadcast a message to your users.</p>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="space-y-3">
          {items.map(item => {
            const meta = TYPE_META[item.type] ?? TYPE_META.info;
            const TypeIcon = meta.icon;
            return (
              <div
                key={item.id}
                className={`rounded-xl border bg-slate-800 overflow-hidden transition-all ${
                  item.isActive ? `${meta.border}` : 'border-slate-700 opacity-60'
                }`}
              >
                <div className="flex items-start gap-4 p-4">
                  {/* Type icon */}
                  <div className={`flex h-9 w-9 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-lg mt-0.5 ${meta.bg}`}>
                    <TypeIcon className={`h-4 w-4 ${meta.color}`} />
                  </div>

                  {/* Content */}
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
                      <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-white truncate">{item.title}</span>
                      <span className={`rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium ${meta.border} ${meta.bg} ${meta.color}`}>
                        {meta.label}
                      </span>
                      <span className="rounded-full border border-slate-600 bg-slate-700/50 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium text-slate-400">
                        {AUDIENCE_LABELS[item.targetAudience]}
                      </span>
                      {!item.isActive && (
                        <span className="rounded-full border border-slate-600 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium text-slate-500">
                          Inactive
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-xs text-slate-300 mt-1.5 leading-relaxed">{item.message}</p>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-2 text-[10px] text-slate-500">
                      <span>By {item.createdBy}</span>
                      <span>·</span>
                      <span>{formatTs(item.createdAt)}</span>
                      {item.expiresAt && (
                        <>
                          <span>·</span>
                          <span>Expires {formatTs(item.expiresAt)}</span>
                        </>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Actions */}
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setConfirmToggle({ id: item.id, current: item.isActive })}
                      disabled={togglingId === item.id}
                      title={item.isActive ? 'Deactivate' : 'Activate'}
                      className="text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
                    >
                      {togglingId === item.id
                        ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />
                        : item.isActive
                        ? <ToggleRight className="h-5 w-5 text-indigo-400" />
                        : <ToggleLeft className="h-5 w-5" />}
                    </button>
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setConfirmDelete(item)}
                      disabled={deletingId === item.id}
                      className="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
                    >
                      {deletingId === item.id
                        ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />
                        : <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />}
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}

      {showCreate && (
        <CreateModal
          adminEmail={adminUser?.email ?? 'admin'}
          onClose={() => setShowCreate(false)}
          onCreated={a => {
            setItems(prev => [a, ...prev]);
            setShowCreate(false);
          }}
        />
      )}

      {/* Toggle confirmation */}
      <ConfirmModal
        isOpen={!!confirmToggle}
        onClose={() => setConfirmToggle(null)}
        onConfirm={executeToggle}
        title={confirmToggle?.current ? 'Deactivate announcement?' : 'Activate announcement?'}
        description={
          confirmToggle?.current
            ? 'The announcement will be hidden from users immediately.'
            : 'The announcement will become visible to users immediately.'
        }
        variant="simple"
        confirmColor={confirmToggle?.current ? 'red' : 'indigo'}
        confirmLabel={confirmToggle?.current ? 'Yes, deactivate' : 'Yes, activate'}
      />

      {/* Delete confirmation */}
      <ConfirmModal
        isOpen={!!confirmDelete}
        onClose={() => setConfirmDelete(null)}
        onConfirm={executeDelete}
        title={`Delete "${confirmDelete?.title ?? 'announcement'}"?`}
        description="This will permanently remove the announcement. This cannot be undone. Type CONFIRM to proceed."
        variant="destructive"
        confirmColor="red"
        confirmLabel="Delete"
      />
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useMemo } from 'react';
import { collection, query, orderBy, onSnapshot, limit } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { format, isWithinInterval, parseISO, startOfDay, endOfDay } from 'date-fns';
import {
  Copy,
  CheckCircle,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronRight,
  ChevronDown,
  ChevronUp,
  Search,
  Download,
  X,
  SlidersHorizontal,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { AuditLog } from '../types';
import SkeletonTable from '../components/SkeletonTable';

const PAGE_SIZE = 50;

// Colour each action type differently for quick scanning
const ACTION_COLORS: Record<string, string> = {
  admin_grant:       'bg-green-500/20 border-green-500/30 text-green-300',
  admin_upgrade:     'bg-indigo-500/20 border-indigo-500/30 text-indigo-300',
  admin_downgrade:   'bg-orange-500/20 border-orange-500/30 text-orange-300',
  admin_extend:      'bg-blue-500/20 border-blue-500/30 text-blue-300',
  admin_cancel:      'bg-red-500/20 border-red-500/30 text-red-300',
  admin_override:    'bg-yellow-500/20 border-yellow-500/30 text-yellow-300',
  admin_reset_trial: 'bg-violet-500/20 border-violet-500/30 text-violet-300',
  payment_success:   'bg-green-500/20 border-green-500/30 text-green-300',
  manual_payment:    'bg-cyan-500/20 border-cyan-500/30 text-cyan-300',
  payment_failed:    'bg-red-500/20 border-red-500/30 text-red-300',
  auto_grace:        'bg-amber-500/20 border-amber-500/30 text-amber-300',
  auto_expire:       'bg-pink-500/20 border-pink-500/30 text-pink-300',
};

function actionBadgeClass(action: string) {
  return ACTION_COLORS[action] ?? 'bg-slate-600/40 border-slate-500/30 text-slate-300';
}

export default function AuditPage() {
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<AuditLog[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [expandedId, setExpandedId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [copiedId, setCopiedId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Filters
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [actionFilter, setActionFilter] = useState('all');
  const [performedByFilter, setPerformedByFilter] = useState('all');
  const [dateFrom, setDateFrom] = useState('');
  const [dateTo, setDateTo] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const unsubscribe = onSnapshot(
      query(
        collection(db, 'subscription_logs'),
        orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'),
        limit(1000)
      ),
      (snap) => {
        setLogs(snap.docs.map(d => ({ id: d.id, ...(d.data() as Omit<AuditLog, 'id'>) })));
        setLoading(false);
      },
      (err) => {
        console.error('Error loading audit logs:', err);
        setLoading(false);
      }
    );
    return unsubscribe;
  }, []);

  // Derive unique action list from loaded data
  const ACTIONS = useMemo(
    () => ['all', ...Array.from(new Set(logs.map(l => l.action))).sort()],
    [logs]
  );

  const hasActiveFilters =
    search !== '' ||
    actionFilter !== 'all' ||
    performedByFilter !== 'all' ||
    dateFrom !== '' ||
    dateTo !== '';

  function clearFilters() {
    setSearch('');
    setActionFilter('all');
    setPerformedByFilter('all');
    setDateFrom('');
    setDateTo('');
    setPage(1);
  }

  function formatTs(ts: any): string {
    if (!ts) return '—';
    try { return format(ts.toDate(), 'MMM d, yyyy HH:mm:ss'); } catch { return '—'; }
  }

  function copyUid(uid: string) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(uid);
    setCopiedId(uid);
    setTimeout(() => setCopiedId(null), 1500);
  }

  const filtered = useMemo(() => {
    return logs.filter(l => {
      if (actionFilter !== 'all' && l.action !== actionFilter) return false;
      if (performedByFilter !== 'all' && l.performedBy !== performedByFilter) return false;

      if (search) {
        const q = search.toLowerCase();
        const matchUid = l.userId?.toLowerCase().includes(q);
        const matchBy = String(l.performedBy ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q);
        const matchAction = l.action?.toLowerCase().includes(q);
        if (!matchUid && !matchBy && !matchAction) return false;
      }

      if (dateFrom || dateTo) {
        let ts: Date | null = null;
        try { ts = l.timestamp?.toDate?.() ?? null; } catch { ts = null; }
        if (!ts) return false;
        if (dateFrom) {
          try { if (ts < startOfDay(parseISO(dateFrom))) return false; } catch {}
        }
        if (dateTo) {
          try { if (ts > endOfDay(parseISO(dateTo))) return false; } catch {}
        }
      }

      return true;
    });
  }, [logs, search, actionFilter, performedByFilter, dateFrom, dateTo]);

  const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(filtered.length / PAGE_SIZE));
  const pageLogs = filtered.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_SIZE, page * PAGE_SIZE);

  // CSV export of filtered results
  function exportCSV() {
    const header = ['Timestamp', 'User ID', 'Action', 'Performed By', 'Previous State', 'New State'];
    const rows = filtered.map(l => [
      formatTs(l.timestamp),
      l.userId ?? '',
      l.action ?? '',
      String(l.performedBy ?? ''),
      JSON.stringify(l.previousState ?? null),
      JSON.stringify(l.newState ?? {}),
    ]);
    const csv = [header, ...rows]
      .map(r => r.map(v => `"${String(v).replace(/"/g, '""')}"`).join(','))
      .join('\n');
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = `audit_log_${format(new Date(), 'yyyyMMdd_HHmm')}.csv`;
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4 flex-wrap">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Audit Log</h1>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">Immutable subscription event trail · last 1 000 entries</p>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={exportCSV}
          disabled={loading || filtered.length === 0}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3.5 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-700 hover:text-white disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
        >
          <Download className="h-4 w-4" />
          Export CSV
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Filter bar */}
      <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-4 space-y-3">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
          <SlidersHorizontal className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-slate-400" />
          <span className="text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Filters</span>
          {hasActiveFilters && (
            <button
              onClick={clearFilters}
              className="ml-auto flex items-center gap-1 rounded-md border border-slate-600 bg-slate-700 px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-600 transition-colors"
            >
              <X className="h-3 w-3" /> Clear all
            </button>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Row 1: search + action + actor */}
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
          {/* Search */}
          <div className="relative flex-1 min-w-52">
            <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-4 w-4 text-slate-400 pointer-events-none" />
            <input
              type="text"
              value={search}
              onChange={e => { setSearch(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
              placeholder="Search user ID, action, or actor…"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 pl-9 pr-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
            {search && (
              <button onClick={() => { setSearch(''); setPage(1); }} className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300">
                <X className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
              </button>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Action */}
          <select
            value={actionFilter}
            onChange={e => { setActionFilter(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
            className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
          >
            {ACTIONS.map(a => (
              <option key={a} value={a}>
                {a === 'all' ? 'All Actions' : a.replace(/_/g, ' ')}
              </option>
            ))}
          </select>

          {/* Actor */}
          <select
            value={performedByFilter}
            onChange={e => { setPerformedByFilter(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
            className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
          >
            <option value="all">All Actors</option>
            <option value="admin">Admin</option>
            <option value="system">System</option>
          </select>
        </div>

        {/* Row 2: date range */}
        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3">
          <span className="text-xs text-slate-500 shrink-0">Date range</span>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-1 flex-wrap">
            <input
              type="date"
              value={dateFrom}
              onChange={e => { setDateFrom(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
              className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500 [color-scheme:dark]"
            />
            <span className="text-slate-500 text-xs">to</span>
            <input
              type="date"
              value={dateTo}
              min={dateFrom || undefined}
              onChange={e => { setDateTo(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
              className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500 [color-scheme:dark]"
            />
          </div>
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-400 shrink-0">
            <span className="font-medium text-white">{filtered.length}</span> entr{filtered.length === 1 ? 'y' : 'ies'}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {loading ? (
        <SkeletonTable rows={12} cols={5} />
      ) : (
        <>
          <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
              <table className="w-full text-sm">
                <thead>
                  <tr className="bg-slate-800 border-b border-slate-700 sticky top-0">
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">User ID</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Action</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Performed By</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Timestamp</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Details</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/40">
                  {pageLogs.length === 0 ? (
                    <tr>
                      <td colSpan={5} className="py-16 text-center">
                        <p className="text-slate-500 text-sm">No entries match your filters</p>
                        {hasActiveFilters && (
                          <button
                            onClick={clearFilters}
                            className="mt-3 text-xs text-indigo-400 hover:text-indigo-300 underline underline-offset-2"
                          >
                            Clear all filters
                          </button>
                        )}
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  ) : pageLogs.map((log, i) => (
                    <React.Fragment key={log.id}>
                      <tr
                        className={`${i % 2 === 0 ? 'bg-slate-800' : 'bg-slate-800/50'} hover:bg-slate-700/50 cursor-pointer transition-colors`}
                        onClick={() => setExpandedId(expandedId === log.id ? null : log.id)}
                      >
                        <td className="px-4 py-3">
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <span className="font-mono text-xs text-slate-300">{log.userId?.slice(0, 12)}…</span>
                            <button
                              onClick={e => { e.stopPropagation(); copyUid(log.userId); }}
                              className="text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 transition-colors"
                            >
                              {copiedId === log.userId
                                ? <CheckCircle className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-400" />
                                : <Copy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
                            </button>
                          </div>
                        </td>
                        <td className="px-4 py-3">
                          <span className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium capitalize ${actionBadgeClass(log.action)}`}>
                            {log.action?.replace(/_/g, ' ')}
                          </span>
                        </td>
                        <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono truncate max-w-32" title={String(log.performedBy ?? '')}>
                          {String(log.performedBy ?? '—')}
                        </td>
                        <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400 whitespace-nowrap">{formatTs(log.timestamp)}</td>
                        <td className="px-4 py-3">
                          {expandedId === log.id
                            ? <ChevronUp className="h-4 w-4 text-slate-400" />
                            : <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4 text-slate-400" />}
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                      {expandedId === log.id && (
                        <tr className="bg-slate-900 border-b border-slate-700">
                          <td colSpan={5} className="px-4 py-4">
                            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                              <div>
                                <p className="text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-2 uppercase tracking-wider">Previous State</p>
                                <pre className="text-xs text-slate-300 bg-slate-800 rounded-lg p-3 overflow-auto max-h-48 border border-slate-700">
                                  {log.previousState
                                    ? JSON.stringify(log.previousState, null, 2)
                                    : 'null'}
                                </pre>
                              </div>
                              <div>
                                <p className="text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-2 uppercase tracking-wider">New State</p>
                                <pre className="text-xs text-slate-300 bg-slate-800 rounded-lg p-3 overflow-auto max-h-48 border border-slate-700">
                                  {JSON.stringify(log.newState, null, 2)}
                                </pre>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      )}
                    </React.Fragment>
                  ))}
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Pagination */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm text-slate-400">
            <span>{filtered.length} entries • Page {page} of {totalPages}</span>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <button
                onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.max(1, p - 1))}
                disabled={page === 1}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
              >
                <ChevronLeft className="h-4 w-4" /> Prev
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.min(totalPages, p + 1))}
                disabled={page === totalPages}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
              >
                Next <ChevronRight className="h-4 w-4" />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { doc, getDoc, setDoc, Timestamp } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { format } from 'date-fns';
import { Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { GlobalConfig } from '../types';
import { useToast } from '../components/Toast';

const DEFAULT_CONFIG: GlobalConfig = {
  freeTrialEnabled: true,
  trialDurationDays: 14,
  defaultPlan: 'free',
  gracePeriodDays: 3,
  appMode: 'hybrid',
};

export default function ConfigPage() {
  const { showToast } = useToast();
  const [config, setConfig] = useState<GlobalConfig>(DEFAULT_CONFIG);
  const [updatedAt, setUpdatedAt] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      try {
        const snap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'config', 'global'));
        if (snap.exists()) {
          const data = snap.data();
          setConfig({
            freeTrialEnabled: data.freeTrialEnabled ?? DEFAULT_CONFIG.freeTrialEnabled,
            trialDurationDays: data.trialDurationDays ?? DEFAULT_CONFIG.trialDurationDays,
            defaultPlan: data.defaultPlan ?? DEFAULT_CONFIG.defaultPlan,
            gracePeriodDays: data.gracePeriodDays ?? DEFAULT_CONFIG.gracePeriodDays,
            appMode: data.appMode ?? DEFAULT_CONFIG.appMode,
          });
          setUpdatedAt(data.updatedAt);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(err);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
    load();
  }, []);

  async function handleSave() {
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      await setDoc(doc(db, 'config', 'global'), {
        ...config,
        updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
      }, { merge: true });
      setUpdatedAt(Timestamp.now());
      showToast('Configuration saved', 'success');
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Failed to save config', 'error');
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  function formatTs(ts: any): string {
    if (!ts) return 'Never';
    try { return format(ts.toDate(), 'MMM d, yyyy HH:mm'); } catch { return '—'; }
  }

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-4 max-w-2xl">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Global Config</h1>
        <div className="h-80 rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 animate-pulse" />
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6 max-w-2xl">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Global Config</h1>
        <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">
          Platform-wide settings. Last updated: <span className="text-slate-300">{formatTs(updatedAt)}</span>
        </p>
      </div>

      <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 overflow-hidden">
        <div className="p-6 space-y-6">
          {/* Free Trial Toggle */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <label className="text-sm font-medium text-white">Free Trial Enabled</label>
              <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-0.5">Allow new users to start a free trial</p>
            </div>
            <button
              onClick={() => setConfig(c => ({ ...c, freeTrialEnabled: !c.freeTrialEnabled }))}
              className={`relative inline-flex h-6 w-11 items-center rounded-full transition-colors ${
                config.freeTrialEnabled ? 'bg-indigo-600' : 'bg-slate-600'
              }`}
            >
              <span
                className={`inline-block h-4 w-4 transform rounded-full bg-white transition-transform shadow-sm ${
                  config.freeTrialEnabled ? 'translate-x-6' : 'translate-x-1'
                }`}
              />
            </button>
          </div>

          <hr className="border-slate-700" />

          {/* Trial Duration */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-white mb-1.5">Trial Duration (days)</label>
            <input
              type="number"
              min={1}
              value={config.trialDurationDays}
              onChange={e => setConfig(c => ({ ...c, trialDurationDays: Number(e.target.value) }))}
              className="w-32 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>

          {/* Grace Period */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-white mb-1.5">Grace Period (days)</label>
            <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mb-2">Days after expiry before access is fully revoked</p>
            <input
              type="number"
              min={0}
              value={config.gracePeriodDays}
              onChange={e => setConfig(c => ({ ...c, gracePeriodDays: Number(e.target.value) }))}
              className="w-32 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>

          {/* Default Plan */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-white mb-1.5">Default Plan</label>
            <select
              value={config.defaultPlan}
              onChange={e => setConfig(c => ({ ...c, defaultPlan: e.target.value }))}
              className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            >
              <option value="free">Free</option>
              <option value="pro">Pro</option>
              <option value="enterprise">Enterprise</option>
            </select>
          </div>

          {/* App Mode */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-white mb-3">App Mode</label>
            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
              {(['free', 'paid', 'hybrid'] as const).map(mode => (
                <label key={mode} className="flex items-center gap-3 cursor-pointer">
                  <div
                    className={`flex h-4 w-4 items-center justify-center rounded-full border-2 transition-colors ${
                      config.appMode === mode
                        ? 'border-indigo-500 bg-indigo-500'
                        : 'border-slate-600 bg-transparent'
                    }`}
                    onClick={() => setConfig(c => ({ ...c, appMode: mode }))}
                  >
                    {config.appMode === mode && (
                      <div className="h-1.5 w-1.5 rounded-full bg-white" />
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-sm text-slate-300 capitalize">{mode}</span>
                </label>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="px-6 py-4 border-t border-slate-700 flex justify-end">
          <button
            onClick={handleSave}
            disabled={saving}
            className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 px-6 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-50 transition-colors"
          >
            {saving && <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />}
            Save Config
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

[END: artifacts\admin-panel\src\pages\ConfigPage.tsx]

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { Link, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import {
  collection,
  collectionGroup,
  getDocs,
  query,
  orderBy,
  limit,
  where,
  Timestamp,
} from 'firebase/firestore';
import {
  AreaChart,
  Area,
  XAxis,
  YAxis,
  CartesianGrid,
  Tooltip,
  ResponsiveContainer,
} from 'recharts';
import {
  format,
  subDays,
  subMonths,
  startOfMonth,
  endOfMonth,
  isWithinInterval,
  startOfDay,
  parseISO,
} from 'date-fns';
import {
  TrendingUp,
  AlertTriangle,
  AlertCircle,
  Activity,
  IndianRupee,
  Gift,
  Megaphone,
  Users,
  RefreshCw,
  ArrowRight,
  Crown,
  Clock,
  XCircle,
  Zap,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { AuditLog, Plan } from '../types';

// ─── types ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

interface Stats {
  activeCount: number;
  freeCount: number;
  expiredGraceCount: number;
  expiringCount: number;
  recentChanges: number;
  recentGrants: number;
  activeAnnouncements: number;
  currentMonthRevenue: number;
}

interface DayBucket {
  date: string;   // 'Apr 1'
  isoDate: string; // '2025-04-01' for tooltip
  events: number;
  grants: number;
  cancels: number;
}

interface MonthBar {
  label: string;
  revenue: number;
  count: number;
}

// ─── Action badge ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const ACTION_STYLE: Record<string, string> = {
  grant:             'bg-green-500/20 border-green-500/30 text-green-300',
  upgrade:           'bg-indigo-500/20 border-indigo-500/30 text-indigo-300',
  downgrade:         'bg-orange-500/20 border-orange-500/30 text-orange-300',
  extend:            'bg-blue-500/20 border-blue-500/30 text-blue-300',
  cancel:            'bg-red-500/20 border-red-500/30 text-red-300',
  admin_override:    'bg-yellow-500/20 border-yellow-500/30 text-yellow-300',
  admin_reset_trial: 'bg-violet-500/20 border-violet-500/30 text-violet-300',
};
function actionStyle(action: string) {
  return ACTION_STYLE[action] ?? 'bg-slate-600/30 border-slate-600/40 text-slate-300';
}

// ─── Stat card ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

interface StatCardProps {
  label: string;
  value: number | string;
  icon: React.ElementType;
  iconColor: string;
  iconBg: string;
  href?: string;
  formatter?: (v: number) => string;
  loading: boolean;
}

function StatCard({ label, value, icon: Icon, iconColor, iconBg, href, loading }: StatCardProps) {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const clickable = !!href;
  return (
    <div
      className={`rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-5 transition-colors ${
        clickable ? 'cursor-pointer hover:border-slate-500 hover:bg-slate-750' : ''
      }`}
      onClick={clickable ? () => navigate(href!) : undefined}
    >
      {loading ? (
        <>
          <div className="h-3.5 w-28 bg-slate-700 rounded animate-pulse mb-4" />
          <div className="h-8 w-16 bg-slate-700 rounded animate-pulse" />
        </>
      ) : (
        <>
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
            <p className="text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wide">{label}</p>
            <div className={`rounded-lg p-2 ${iconBg}`}>
              <Icon className={`h-4 w-4 ${iconColor}`} />
            </div>
          </div>
          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-white tabular-nums">
            {typeof value === 'number' ? value.toLocaleString('en-IN') : value}
          </p>
          {clickable && (
            <p className="mt-2 text-[10px] text-slate-500 flex items-center gap-1 group-hover:text-slate-400">
              View details <ArrowRight className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
            </p>
          )}
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── Custom tooltip for area chart ───────────────────────────────────────────

function DayTooltip({ active, payload, label }: any) {
  if (!active || !payload?.length) return null;
  return (
    <div className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-2.5 shadow-xl text-xs">
      <p className="font-semibold text-white mb-1.5">{label}</p>
      {payload.map((p: any) => (
        <p key={p.dataKey} style={{ color: p.color }} className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className="inline-block h-2 w-2 rounded-full" style={{ background: p.color }} />
          {p.name}: <span className="font-semibold text-white">{p.value}</span>
        </p>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── Activity chart ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function ActivityChart({ days, loading }: { days: DayBucket[]; loading: boolean }) {
  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-5 h-64 animate-pulse" />
    );
  }
  const hasData = days.some(d => d.events > 0);
  return (
    <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-5">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-base font-semibold text-white">Subscription Activity</h2>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-0.5">Daily events — last 30 days</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-[10px] text-slate-400">
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <span className="inline-block h-2 w-2 rounded-full bg-indigo-400" /> All events
          </span>
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <span className="inline-block h-2 w-2 rounded-full bg-green-400" /> Grants
          </span>
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <span className="inline-block h-2 w-2 rounded-full bg-red-400" /> Cancels
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>
      {!hasData ? (
        <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-44 text-sm text-slate-500">
          No activity in the last 30 days
        </div>
      ) : (
        <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={180}>
          <AreaChart data={days} margin={{ top: 4, right: 0, left: -20, bottom: 0 }}>
            <defs>
              <linearGradient id="gradEvents" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                <stop offset="5%" stopColor="#6366f1" stopOpacity={0.3} />
                <stop offset="95%" stopColor="#6366f1" stopOpacity={0} />
              </linearGradient>
              <linearGradient id="gradGrants" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                <stop offset="5%" stopColor="#4ade80" stopOpacity={0.25} />
                <stop offset="95%" stopColor="#4ade80" stopOpacity={0} />
              </linearGradient>
              <linearGradient id="gradCancels" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                <stop offset="5%" stopColor="#f87171" stopOpacity={0.2} />
                <stop offset="95%" stopColor="#f87171" stopOpacity={0} />
              </linearGradient>
            </defs>
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#334155" vertical={false} />
            <XAxis
              dataKey="date"
              tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: '#94a3b8' }}
              tickLine={false}
              axisLine={false}
              interval="preserveStartEnd"
            />
            <YAxis
              tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: '#94a3b8' }}
              tickLine={false}
              axisLine={false}
              allowDecimals={false}
            />
            <Tooltip content={<DayTooltip />} />
            <Area
              type="monotone"
              dataKey="events"
              name="All events"
              stroke="#6366f1"
              strokeWidth={2}
              fill="url(#gradEvents)"
              dot={false}
              activeDot={{ r: 4, fill: '#6366f1' }}
            />
            <Area
              type="monotone"
              dataKey="grants"
              name="Grants"
              stroke="#4ade80"
              strokeWidth={1.5}
              fill="url(#gradGrants)"
              dot={false}
              activeDot={{ r: 3, fill: '#4ade80' }}
            />
            <Area
              type="monotone"
              dataKey="cancels"
              name="Cancels"
              stroke="#f87171"
              strokeWidth={1.5}
              fill="url(#gradCancels)"
              dot={false}
              activeDot={{ r: 3, fill: '#f87171' }}
            />
          </AreaChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── Revenue bar chart ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function RevenueChart({ bars, loading }: { bars: MonthBar[]; loading: boolean }) {
  if (loading) return <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-5 h-56 animate-pulse" />;
  const max = Math.max(...bars.map(b => b.revenue), 1);
  const hasData = bars.some(b => b.revenue > 0);
  return (
    <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-5">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-base font-semibold text-white">Monthly Revenue</h2>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-0.5">Last 6 months · paid subscriptions</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-green-500/10">
          <IndianRupee className="h-4 w-4 text-green-400" />
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className="flex items-end gap-3 h-40">
        {bars.map((bar, i) => {
          const heightPct = max === 0 ? 0 : (bar.revenue / max) * 100;
          const isCurrentMonth = i === bars.length - 1;
          return (
            <div key={bar.label} className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2 flex-1 h-full justify-end group relative">
              <div className="absolute bottom-full mb-2 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 hidden group-hover:flex flex-col items-center pointer-events-none z-10">
                <div className="rounded-lg bg-slate-700 border border-slate-600 px-3 py-2 text-center shadow-xl whitespace-nowrap">
                  <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-white">₹{bar.revenue.toLocaleString('en-IN')}</p>
                  <p className="text-[10px] text-slate-400">{bar.count} payment{bar.count !== 1 ? 's' : ''}</p>
                </div>
                <div className="w-2 h-2 rotate-45 bg-slate-700 border-r border-b border-slate-600 -mt-1" />
              </div>
              <div
                className={`w-full rounded-t-md transition-all duration-500 ${
                  isCurrentMonth ? 'bg-indigo-500 group-hover:bg-indigo-400' : 'bg-slate-600 group-hover:bg-slate-500'
                }`}
                style={{ height: `${Math.max(heightPct, bar.revenue > 0 ? 4 : 0)}%` }}
              />
              <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-medium">{bar.label}</span>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
      {!hasData && (
        <p className="text-center text-xs text-slate-500 mt-4">
          Revenue will appear here once paid subscriptions are recorded with plan prices.
        </p>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── Subscription Health widget ─────────────────────────────────────────────

interface HealthCounts {
  totalActive: number;
  totalTrial: number;
  inGracePeriod: number;
  expiredToday: number;
  freeUsers: number;
}

function SubscriptionHealthWidget() {
  const [counts, setCounts] = useState<HealthCounts | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [lastUpdated, setLastUpdated] = useState<Date | null>(null);
  const [spinning, setSpinning] = useState(false);

  const fetchHealth = useCallback(async (isManual = false) => {
    if (isManual) setSpinning(true);
    else setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const now = new Date();
      const yesterday = new Date(now.getTime() - 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
      const snap = await getDocs(collectionGroup(db, 'subscription'));

      let totalActive = 0, totalTrial = 0, inGracePeriod = 0;
      let expiredToday = 0, freeUsers = 0;

      snap.forEach(doc => {
        // Per spec: only 'current' sub-docs
        if (doc.ref.id !== 'current') return;
        const d = doc.data();
        const status: string = d.status ?? '';
        const plan: string  = d.planId ?? d.plan ?? '';

        // a. Active Pro — active, not free, endDate > now
        if (status === 'active' && plan !== 'free') {
          try { if ((d.endDate?.toDate?.() ?? new Date(0)) > now) totalActive++; } catch {}
        }

        // b. On Trial — trial, endDate > now
        if (status === 'trial') {
          try { if ((d.endDate?.toDate?.() ?? new Date(0)) > now) totalTrial++; } catch {}
        }

        // c. Grace Period — expired, graceEndDate > now
        if (status === 'expired') {
          try {
            const grace: Date | null = d.graceEndDate?.toDate?.() ?? null;
            const end: Date | null   = d.endDate?.toDate?.() ?? null;

            if (grace && grace > now) {
              inGracePeriod++;
            } else if (end && end >= yesterday && end <= now && (!grace || grace <= now)) {
              // d. Expired Today — endDate in last 24 h, grace absent or also passed
              expiredToday++;
            }
          } catch {}
        }

        // e. Free Plan — plan === 'free' regardless of status
        if (plan === 'free') freeUsers++;
      });

      setCounts({ totalActive, totalTrial, inGracePeriod, expiredToday, freeUsers });
      setLastUpdated(new Date());
    } catch {
      setError('Could not load subscription data. Check Firestore rules.');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
      setSpinning(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => { fetchHealth(); }, [fetchHealth]);

  const TILES = [
    {
      label: 'Active Pro',
      value: counts?.totalActive ?? 0,
      icon: Crown,
      iconColor: 'text-emerald-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-emerald-500/10',
      border: 'border-emerald-500/20',
      numColor: 'text-emerald-300',
    },
    {
      label: 'On Trial',
      value: counts?.totalTrial ?? 0,
      icon: Clock,
      iconColor: 'text-violet-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-violet-500/10',
      border: 'border-violet-500/20',
      numColor: 'text-violet-300',
    },
    {
      label: 'Grace Period',
      value: counts?.inGracePeriod ?? 0,
      icon: AlertTriangle,
      iconColor: 'text-amber-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-amber-500/10',
      border: 'border-amber-500/20',
      numColor: 'text-amber-300',
    },
    {
      label: 'Expired Today',
      value: counts?.expiredToday ?? 0,
      icon: XCircle,
      iconColor: 'text-red-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-red-500/10',
      border: 'border-red-500/20',
      numColor: 'text-red-300',
    },
    {
      label: 'Free Plan',
      value: counts?.freeUsers ?? 0,
      icon: Zap,
      iconColor: 'text-slate-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-slate-600/30',
      border: 'border-slate-600/40',
      numColor: 'text-slate-300',
    },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-5">
      {/* Section header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-base font-semibold text-white">Subscription Health</h2>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-0.5">Live snapshot of all user subscription states</p>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => fetchHealth(true)}
          disabled={spinning || loading}
          className="flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-700 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-600 hover:text-white transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
          title="Refresh subscription health"
        >
          <RefreshCw className={`h-3.5 w-3.5 ${spinning ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
          Refresh
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Error state */}
      {error && (
        <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg border border-red-500/30 bg-red-500/10 px-4 py-3">
          <p className="text-xs text-red-400">{error}</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Tiles — horizontal scroll on mobile, 5-col grid on desktop */}
      <div className="flex gap-3 overflow-x-auto pb-1 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-5 xl:overflow-visible xl:pb-0">
        {TILES.map(tile => (
          <div
            key={tile.label}
            className={`shrink-0 w-40 xl:w-auto rounded-xl border ${tile.border} bg-slate-800/60 p-4 flex flex-col gap-3 transition-colors hover:bg-slate-700/40`}
          >
            {loading ? (
              <>
                <div className="h-8 w-8 rounded-lg bg-slate-700 animate-pulse" />
                <div className="h-7 w-10 bg-slate-700 rounded animate-pulse" />
                <div className="h-3 w-20 bg-slate-700 rounded animate-pulse" />
              </>
            ) : (
              <>
                <div className={`flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center rounded-lg ${tile.iconBg}`}>
                  <tile.icon className={`h-4.5 w-4.5 ${tile.iconColor}`} />
                </div>
                <p className={`text-3xl font-bold tabular-nums ${tile.numColor}`}>
                  {tile.value.toLocaleString('en-IN')}
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs font-medium text-slate-400">{tile.label}</p>
              </>
            )}
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Last updated */}
      {lastUpdated && !loading && (
        <p className="mt-3 text-[10px] text-slate-600">
          Last updated: {format(lastUpdated, 'h:mm a')}
        </p>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── Recent activity table ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function formatTs(ts: any): string {
  try { return format(ts.toDate(), 'MMM d, HH:mm'); } catch { return '—'; }
}

function ActivityTable({ logs, loading }: { logs: AuditLog[]; loading: boolean }) {
  return (
    <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-4 border-b border-slate-700">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-base font-semibold text-white">Recent Activity</h2>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-0.5">Last 20 subscription events</p>
        </div>
        <Link
          to="/audit"
          className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs text-indigo-400 hover:text-indigo-300 transition-colors"
        >
          Full log <ArrowRight className="h-3 w-3" />
        </Link>
      </div>
      {loading ? (
        <div className="divide-y divide-slate-700/50">
          {Array.from({ length: 6 }).map((_, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="flex items-center gap-4 px-5 py-3">
              <div className="h-3 w-24 bg-slate-700 rounded animate-pulse" />
              <div className="h-3 w-20 bg-slate-700 rounded animate-pulse" />
              <div className="h-3 w-16 bg-slate-700 rounded animate-pulse ml-auto" />
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      ) : logs.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="py-12 text-center text-slate-500 text-sm">No activity yet</div>
      ) : (
        <div className="overflow-x-auto">
          <table className="w-full text-sm">
            <thead>
              <tr className="border-b border-slate-700 bg-slate-800/50">
                <th className="px-5 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">User</th>
                <th className="px-5 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Action</th>
                <th className="px-5 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">By</th>
                <th className="px-5 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Time</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/40">
              {logs.map((log, i) => (
                <tr key={log.id} className={i % 2 === 0 ? 'bg-slate-800' : 'bg-slate-800/50'}>
                  <td className="px-5 py-3">
                    <Link
                      to={`/users/${log.userId}`}
                      className="font-mono text-xs text-indigo-400 hover:text-indigo-300 transition-colors"
                      title={log.userId}
                    >
                      {log.userId?.slice(0, 12)}…
                    </Link>
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-5 py-3">
                    <span className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium capitalize ${actionStyle(log.action)}`}>
                      {log.action?.replace(/_/g, ' ')}
                    </span>
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-5 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400 capitalize">{log.performedBy}</td>
                  <td className="px-5 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400 whitespace-nowrap">{formatTs(log.timestamp)}</td>
                </tr>
              ))}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── Main page ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export default function DashboardPage() {
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<Stats | null>(null);
  const [activity, setActivity] = useState<AuditLog[]>([]);
  const [dayBuckets, setDayBuckets] = useState<DayBucket[]>([]);
  const [revenueBars, setRevenueBars] = useState<MonthBar[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [refreshing, setRefreshing] = useState(false);
  const [lastRefreshed, setLastRefreshed] = useState<Date | null>(null);

  const load = useCallback(async (isRefresh = false) => {
    if (isRefresh) setRefreshing(true);
    else setLoading(true);

    try {
      const now = new Date();
      const in3Days = new Date(now.getTime() + 3 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
      const thirtyDaysAgo = subDays(now, 30);
      const sevenDaysAgo = subDays(now, 7);

      const [subSnap, logsRecentSnap, logs30dSnap, plansSnap, announcementsSnap] =
        await Promise.all([
          getDocs(collectionGroup(db, 'subscription')),
          getDocs(query(
            collection(db, 'subscription_logs'),
            orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'),
            limit(20),
          )),
          getDocs(query(
            collection(db, 'subscription_logs'),
            where('timestamp', '>=', Timestamp.fromDate(thirtyDaysAgo)),
          )),
          getDocs(collection(db, 'plans')),
          getDocs(query(
            collection(db, 'announcements'),
            where('isActive', '==', true),
          )),
        ]);

      // Plan price map for revenue
      const planMap: Record<string, Plan> = {};
      plansSnap.forEach(d => { planMap[d.id] = { id: d.id, ...(d.data() as Omit<Plan, 'id'>) }; });

      // 30-day buckets keyed by 'yyyy-MM-dd'
      const bucketMap: Record<string, DayBucket> = {};
      for (let i = 29; i >= 0; i--) {
        const d = subDays(now, i);
        const iso = format(d, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        const label = format(d, 'MMM d');
        bucketMap[iso] = { date: label, isoDate: iso, events: 0, grants: 0, cancels: 0 };
      }

      // Revenue — last 6 months
      const months: MonthBar[] = Array.from({ length: 6 }, (_, i) => {
        const d = subMonths(now, 5 - i);
        return { label: format(d, 'MMM'), revenue: 0, count: 0 };
      });
      const monthRanges = Array.from({ length: 6 }, (_, i) => {
        const d = subMonths(now, 5 - i);
        return { start: startOfMonth(d), end: endOfMonth(d) };
      });

      // Subscription stats
      let activeCount = 0, freeCount = 0, expiredGraceCount = 0, expiringCount = 0;
      let currentMonthRevenue = 0;
      const cmStart = startOfMonth(now);
      const cmEnd = endOfMonth(now);

      subSnap.forEach(doc => {
        const data = doc.data();
        const status = data.status;
        const planId = data.planId ?? data.plan ?? '';

        if (status === 'active' || status === 'trial') {
          activeCount++;
          // Expiring soon
          try {
            const end: Date = data.endDate?.toDate?.();
            if (end && end >= now && end <= in3Days) expiringCount++;
          } catch {}
        }
        if (planId === 'free' || status === 'free') freeCount++;
        if (status === 'expired' || status === 'grace') expiredGraceCount++;

        // Revenue buckets
        if (!data.paymentId || data.introOffer) return;
        const price = planMap[planId]?.price ?? 0;
        if (price === 0) return;
        const ts = data.updatedAt ?? data.createdAt;
        if (!ts) return;
        try {
          const d: Date = ts.toDate();
          monthRanges.forEach((range, idx) => {
            if (isWithinInterval(d, range)) {
              months[idx].revenue += price;
              months[idx].count += 1;
            }
          });
          if (isWithinInterval(d, { start: cmStart, end: cmEnd })) {
            currentMonthRevenue += price;
          }
        } catch {}
      });

      // 30-day log stats
      let recentGrants = 0;
      let recentChanges = 0;

      logs30dSnap.forEach(doc => {
        const data = doc.data();
        let ts: Date | null = null;
        try { ts = data.timestamp?.toDate?.() ?? null; } catch {}
        if (!ts) return;

        const iso = format(ts, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        if (bucketMap[iso]) {
          bucketMap[iso].events += 1;
          if (data.action === 'grant') bucketMap[iso].grants += 1;
          if (data.action === 'cancel') bucketMap[iso].cancels += 1;
        }

        if (ts >= sevenDaysAgo) {
          recentChanges++;
          if (data.action === 'grant') recentGrants++;
        }
      });

      // Recent activity table
      const recentLogs: AuditLog[] = logsRecentSnap.docs.map(d => ({
        id: d.id,
        ...(d.data() as Omit<AuditLog, 'id'>),
      }));

      setStats({
        activeCount,
        freeCount,
        expiredGraceCount,
        expiringCount,
        recentChanges,
        recentGrants,
        activeAnnouncements: announcementsSnap.size,
        currentMonthRevenue,
      });
      setActivity(recentLogs);
      setDayBuckets(Object.values(bucketMap));
      setRevenueBars(months);
      setLastRefreshed(new Date());
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('[Dashboard]', err);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
      setRefreshing(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);

  const CARDS_ROW1 = [
    {
      label: 'Active & Trial',
      value: stats?.activeCount ?? 0,
      icon: TrendingUp,
      iconColor: 'text-green-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-green-500/10',
      href: '/users',
    },
    {
      label: 'Expiring ≤ 3 Days',
      value: stats?.expiringCount ?? 0,
      icon: AlertTriangle,
      iconColor: 'text-orange-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-orange-500/10',
      href: '/users',
    },
    {
      label: 'Expired / Grace',
      value: stats?.expiredGraceCount ?? 0,
      icon: AlertCircle,
      iconColor: 'text-red-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-red-500/10',
      href: '/users',
    },
    {
      label: 'Free Plan Users',
      value: stats?.freeCount ?? 0,
      icon: Users,
      iconColor: 'text-blue-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-blue-500/10',
      href: '/users',
    },
  ];

  const CARDS_ROW2 = [
    {
      label: 'Changes (7 Days)',
      value: stats?.recentChanges ?? 0,
      icon: Activity,
      iconColor: 'text-indigo-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-indigo-500/10',
      href: '/audit',
    },
    {
      label: 'Grants (7 Days)',
      value: stats?.recentGrants ?? 0,
      icon: Gift,
      iconColor: 'text-violet-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-violet-500/10',
      href: '/giveaway-log',
    },
    {
      label: 'Active Announcements',
      value: stats?.activeAnnouncements ?? 0,
      icon: Megaphone,
      iconColor: 'text-green-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-green-500/10',
      href: '/announcements',
    },
    {
      label: 'Revenue This Month',
      value: stats ? `₹${(stats.currentMonthRevenue).toLocaleString('en-IN')}` : '₹0',
      icon: IndianRupee,
      iconColor: 'text-emerald-400',
      iconBg: 'bg-emerald-500/10',
    },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Dashboard</h1>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">
            {lastRefreshed
              ? `Last updated ${format(lastRefreshed, 'HH:mm:ss')}`
              : 'Overview of your subscription platform'}
          </p>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => load(true)}
          disabled={refreshing || loading}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-700 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-medium text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-600 hover:text-white transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          <RefreshCw className={`h-3.5 w-3.5 ${refreshing ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
          Refresh
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Row 1 — subscription health */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
        {CARDS_ROW1.map(card => (
          <StatCard key={card.label} {...card} loading={loading} />
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Row 2 — activity + revenue */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
        {CARDS_ROW2.map(card => (
          <StatCard key={card.label} {...card} loading={loading} />
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Subscription Health */}
      <SubscriptionHealthWidget />

      {/* 30-day area chart */}
      <ActivityChart days={dayBuckets} loading={loading} />

      {/* 6-month revenue bar chart */}
      <RevenueChart bars={revenueBars} loading={loading} />

      {/* Recent activity */}
      <ActivityTable logs={activity} loading={loading} />
    </div>
  );
}
