import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { collection, getDocs, query, orderBy, where } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { format, startOfMonth, isAfter, differenceInDays } from 'date-fns';
import {
  Gift,
  Copy,
  CheckCircle,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronRight,
  Download,
  Users,
  CalendarDays,
  TrendingUp,
  UserCheck,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import SkeletonTable from '../components/SkeletonTable';

interface GrantEntry {
  id: string;
  userId: string;
  planId: string;
  durationDays: number;
  adminEmail: string;
  endDate: any;
  startDate: any;
  timestamp: any;
}

const PAGE_SIZE = 25;

const PLAN_COLORS: Record<string, string> = {
  free: 'bg-slate-500/20 text-slate-400 border-slate-500/30',
  pro: 'bg-indigo-500/20 text-indigo-300 border-indigo-500/30',
  enterprise: 'bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-300 border-amber-500/30',
};

export default function GiveawayLogPage() {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState<GrantEntry[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [planFilter, setPlanFilter] = useState('all');
  const [copiedId, setCopiedId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      try {
        const snap = await getDocs(
          query(
            collection(db, 'subscription_logs'),
            where('action', '==', 'grant'),
            orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'),
          )
        );
        const results: GrantEntry[] = snap.docs.map(d => {
          const data = d.data();
          const ns = data.newState ?? {};
          const durationDays = (() => {
            try {
              const start: Date = ns.startDate?.toDate ? ns.startDate.toDate() : new Date();
              const end: Date = ns.endDate?.toDate ? ns.endDate.toDate() : new Date();
              return Math.max(1, differenceInDays(end, start));
            } catch { return 0; }
          })();
          return {
            id: d.id,
            userId: data.userId ?? '—',
            planId: ns.planId ?? ns.plan ?? '—',
            durationDays,
            adminEmail: ns.adminEmail ?? data.adminEmail ?? 'admin',
            endDate: ns.endDate ?? null,
            startDate: ns.startDate ?? data.timestamp ?? null,
            timestamp: data.timestamp ?? null,
          };
        });
        setEntries(results);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(err);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
    load();
  }, []);

  function formatTs(ts: any, fmt = 'MMM d, yyyy HH:mm'): string {
    if (!ts) return '—';
    try { return format(ts.toDate(), fmt); } catch { return '—'; }
  }

  function copyToClipboard(text: string) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    setCopiedId(text);
    setTimeout(() => setCopiedId(null), 1500);
  }

  function exportCsv() {
    const header = ['User ID', 'Plan', 'Duration (days)', 'Granted By', 'Start Date', 'End Date', 'Timestamp'];
    const rows = filtered.map(e => [
      e.userId,
      e.planId,
      e.durationDays,
      e.adminEmail,
      formatTs(e.startDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
      formatTs(e.endDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
      formatTs(e.timestamp),
    ]);
    const csv = [header, ...rows].map(r => r.join(',')).join('\n');
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = `giveaway-log-${format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd')}.csv`;
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  }

  const filtered = planFilter === 'all' ? entries : entries.filter(e => e.planId === planFilter);
  const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(filtered.length / PAGE_SIZE));
  const pageItems = filtered.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_SIZE, page * PAGE_SIZE);

  // Stats
  const totalGrants = filtered.length;
  const uniqueUsers = new Set(filtered.map(e => e.userId)).size;
  const thisMonthGrants = filtered.filter(e => {
    try { return isAfter(e.timestamp.toDate(), startOfMonth(new Date())); } catch { return false; }
  }).length;
  const avgDays = totalGrants === 0
    ? 0
    : Math.round(filtered.reduce((s, e) => s + e.durationDays, 0) / totalGrants);

  const STAT_CARDS = [
    { label: 'Total Grants', value: totalGrants, icon: Gift, color: 'text-indigo-400', bg: 'bg-indigo-500/10' },
    { label: 'Unique Users', value: uniqueUsers, icon: UserCheck, color: 'text-green-400', bg: 'bg-green-500/10' },
    { label: 'This Month', value: thisMonthGrants, icon: CalendarDays, color: 'text-blue-400', bg: 'bg-blue-500/10' },
    { label: 'Avg Duration', value: `${avgDays}d`, icon: TrendingUp, color: 'text-amber-400', bg: 'bg-amber-500/10' },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Giveaway Log</h1>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">
            Full history of subscriptions granted manually by admins
          </p>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={exportCsv}
          disabled={filtered.length === 0}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-700 hover:text-white disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
        >
          <Download className="h-4 w-4" />
          Export CSV
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Stats */}
      {loading ? (
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
          {Array.from({ length: 4 }).map((_, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="h-24 rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 animate-pulse" />
          ))}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
          {STAT_CARDS.map(card => (
            <div key={card.label} className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-5">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{card.label}</p>
                <div className={`rounded-lg p-2 ${card.bg}`}>
                  <card.icon className={`h-4 w-4 ${card.color}`} />
                </div>
              </div>
              <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{card.value}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Filter */}
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3 items-center">
        <select
          value={planFilter}
          onChange={e => { setPlanFilter(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
          className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
        >
          <option value="all">All Plans</option>
          <option value="pro">Pro</option>
          <option value="enterprise">Enterprise</option>
        </select>
        <span className="text-sm text-slate-400 ml-auto">{filtered.length} grants</span>
      </div>

      {loading ? (
        <SkeletonTable rows={8} cols={6} />
      ) : filtered.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 py-20 text-center">
          <Gift className="h-10 w-10 text-slate-600 mx-auto mb-3" />
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm font-medium">No grants recorded yet</p>
          <p className="text-slate-500 text-xs mt-1">
            Use "Grant Sub" on the Users page to give a user a free subscription.
          </p>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <>
          <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
              <table className="w-full text-sm">
                <thead>
                  <tr className="bg-slate-800 border-b border-slate-700 sticky top-0">
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">User ID</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Plan</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Duration</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Valid Until</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Granted By</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Date</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/40">
                  {pageItems.map((entry, i) => (
                    <tr
                      key={entry.id}
                      className={`${i % 2 === 0 ? 'bg-slate-800' : 'bg-slate-800/50'} hover:bg-slate-700/40 transition-colors`}
                    >
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <span className="font-mono text-xs text-slate-300">{entry.userId.slice(0, 14)}…</span>
                          <button
                            onClick={() => copyToClipboard(entry.userId)}
                            className="text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 transition-colors"
                          >
                            {copiedId === entry.userId
                              ? <CheckCircle className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-400" />
                              : <Copy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <span className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium capitalize ${PLAN_COLORS[entry.planId] ?? PLAN_COLORS.pro}`}>
                          {entry.planId}
                        </span>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-slate-300">
                          <CalendarDays className="h-3 w-3 text-slate-500" />
                          {entry.durationDays} day{entry.durationDays !== 1 ? 's' : ''}
                        </span>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-300">{formatTs(entry.endDate, 'MMM d, yyyy')}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-full border border-indigo-500/30 bg-indigo-500/10 px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium text-indigo-300 max-w-36 truncate">
                          <Users className="h-3 w-3 shrink-0" />
                          <span className="truncate">{entry.adminEmail}</span>
                        </span>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400">{formatTs(entry.timestamp)}</td>
                    </tr>
                  ))}
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Pagination */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm text-slate-400">
            <span>{filtered.length} records · Page {page} of {totalPages}</span>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <button
                onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.max(1, p - 1))}
                disabled={page === 1}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
              >
                <ChevronLeft className="h-4 w-4" /> Prev
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.min(totalPages, p + 1))}
                disabled={page === totalPages}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
              >
                Next <ChevronRight className="h-4 w-4" />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState, FormEvent } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { ShoppingBag, Loader2, Eye, EyeOff } from 'lucide-react';
import { useAuth } from '../context/AuthContext';

function GoogleLogo() {
  return (
    <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
      <path d="M17.64 9.2c0-.637-.057-1.251-.164-1.84H9v3.481h4.844c-.209 1.125-.843 2.078-1.796 2.717v2.258h2.908c1.702-1.567 2.684-3.874 2.684-6.615z" fill="#4285F4"/>
      <path d="M9 18c2.43 0 4.467-.806 5.956-2.18l-2.908-2.259c-.806.54-1.837.86-3.048.86-2.344 0-4.328-1.584-5.036-3.711H.957v2.332A8.997 8.997 0 0 0 9 18z" fill="#34A853"/>
      <path d="M3.964 10.71A5.41 5.41 0 0 1 3.682 9c0-.593.102-1.17.282-1.71V4.958H.957A8.996 8.996 0 0 0 0 9c0 1.452.348 2.827.957 4.042l3.007-2.332z" fill="#FBBC05"/>
      <path d="M9 3.58c1.321 0 2.508.454 3.44 1.345l2.582-2.58C13.463.891 11.426 0 9 0A8.997 8.997 0 0 0 .957 4.958L3.964 6.29C4.672 4.163 6.656 3.58 9 3.58z" fill="#EA4335"/>
    </svg>
  );
}

export default function LoginPage() {
  const { signIn, signInWithGoogle } = useAuth();
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [showPass, setShowPass] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [googleLoading, setGoogleLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  async function handleSubmit(e: FormEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError('');
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await signIn(email, password);
      navigate('/');
    } catch (err: any) {
      const code = err?.code ?? '';
      if (err?.message?.includes('not authorised')) {
        setError('Access denied. You are not authorised to use this panel.');
      } else if (code === 'auth/wrong-password' || code === 'auth/invalid-credential') {
        setError('Incorrect password. Please try again.');
      } else if (code === 'auth/user-not-found') {
        setError('No account found with this email.');
      } else if (code === 'auth/invalid-email') {
        setError('Invalid email address.');
      } else if (code === 'auth/too-many-requests') {
        setError('Too many failed attempts. Please try again later.');
      } else {
        setError(err?.message ?? 'An error occurred. Please try again.');
      }
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  async function handleGoogleSignIn() {
    setError('');
    setGoogleLoading(true);
    try {
      await signInWithGoogle();
      navigate('/');
    } catch (err: any) {
      const code = err?.code ?? '';
      const msg = err?.message ?? '';
      if (msg === 'ACCESS_DENIED') {
        setError('Access denied. Your Google account is not authorised to use this panel. Contact the system administrator.');
      } else if (code === 'auth/popup-closed-by-user' || code === 'auth/cancelled-popup-request') {
        setError('Sign-in cancelled.');
      } else if (code === 'auth/popup-blocked') {
        setError('Popup was blocked. Allow popups for this site and try again.');
      } else if (code === 'auth/account-exists-with-different-credential') {
        setError('An account already exists with this email using a different sign-in method.');
      } else if (code === 'auth/unauthorized-domain') {
        setError('This domain is not authorised in Firebase. Add it to the Firebase Console under Authentication → Authorized domains.');
      } else {
        setError('Sign-in failed. Please try again.');
      }
    } finally {
      setGoogleLoading(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-slate-900 flex items-center justify-center p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center mb-8">
          <div className="flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-indigo-600 mb-4">
            <ShoppingBag className="h-6 w-6 text-white" />
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Shopkeeper Admin</h1>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">Sign in to your admin account</p>
        </div>

        <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-8 shadow-2xl">
          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-300 mb-1.5">
                Email address
              </label>
              <input
                type="email"
                value={email}
                onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                required
                autoComplete="email"
                placeholder="admin@example.com"
                className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500 focus:border-transparent transition"
              />
            </div>

            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-slate-300 mb-1.5">
                Password
              </label>
              <div className="relative">
                <input
                  type={showPass ? 'text' : 'password'}
                  value={password}
                  onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                  required
                  autoComplete="current-password"
                  placeholder="••••••••"
                  className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3.5 py-2.5 pr-10 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500 focus:border-transparent transition"
                />
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => setShowPass(!showPass)}
                  className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-300"
                >
                  {showPass ? <EyeOff className="h-4 w-4" /> : <Eye className="h-4 w-4" />}
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {error && (
              <div className="rounded-lg border border-red-500/30 bg-red-500/10 px-4 py-3">
                <p className="text-sm text-red-400">{error}</p>
              </div>
            )}

            <button
              type="submit"
              disabled={loading || googleLoading}
              className="flex w-full items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 px-4 py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-60 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
            >
              {loading && <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />}
              {loading ? 'Signing in...' : 'Sign In'}
            </button>
          </form>

          {/* Divider */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 my-5">
            <div className="flex-1 h-px bg-slate-700" />
            <span className="text-xs text-slate-500 font-medium uppercase tracking-wider">or</span>
            <div className="flex-1 h-px bg-slate-700" />
          </div>

          {/* Google Sign-In */}
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={handleGoogleSignIn}
            disabled={loading || googleLoading}
            className="flex w-full items-center justify-center gap-3 rounded-lg border border-slate-300 bg-white px-4 py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 disabled:opacity-60 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors shadow-sm"
          >
            {googleLoading
              ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin text-gray-500" />
              : <GoogleLogo />}
            {googleLoading ? 'Signing in...' : 'Continue with Google'}
          </button>
        </div>

        <p className="mt-6 text-center text-xs text-slate-500">
          Admin accounts are created manually. Contact your system administrator for access.
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { collectionGroup, collection, getDocs, query, orderBy, doc, getDoc } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { format, startOfMonth, isAfter } from 'date-fns';
import {
  Download,
  Copy,
  CheckCircle,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronRight,
  TrendingUp,
  IndianRupee,
  Receipt,
  CalendarDays,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { Plan } from '../types';
import SkeletonTable from '../components/SkeletonTable';

interface PaymentRecord {
  uid: string;
  planId: string;
  paymentId: string;
  source: string;
  status: string;
  amount: number;
  paidAt: any;
  introOffer: boolean;
}

const PAGE_SIZE = 25;

const PLAN_COLORS: Record<string, string> = {
  free: 'bg-slate-500/20 text-slate-400 border-slate-500/30',
  pro: 'bg-indigo-500/20 text-indigo-300 border-indigo-500/30',
  enterprise: 'bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-300 border-amber-500/30',
};

export default function PaymentHistoryPage() {
  const [records, setRecords] = useState<PaymentRecord[]>([]);
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState<Record<string, Plan>>({});
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [planFilter, setPlanFilter] = useState('all');
  const [copiedId, setCopiedId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      try {
        const [subSnap, plansSnap] = await Promise.all([
          getDocs(collectionGroup(db, 'subscription')),
          getDocs(collection(db, 'plans')),
        ]);

        const planMap: Record<string, Plan> = {};
        plansSnap.forEach(d => {
          planMap[d.id] = { id: d.id, ...(d.data() as Omit<Plan, 'id'>) };
        });
        setPlans(planMap);

        const results: PaymentRecord[] = [];
        subSnap.forEach(d => {
          const data = d.data();
          const pathParts = d.ref.path.split('/');
          const uid = pathParts[1];
          const planId = data.planId ?? data.plan ?? 'free';
          const paymentId = data.paymentId;
          if (!paymentId) return;
          const price = planMap[planId]?.price ?? 0;
          results.push({
            uid,
            planId,
            paymentId,
            source: data.source ?? '—',
            status: data.status ?? '—',
            amount: data.introOffer ? 0 : price,
            paidAt: data.updatedAt ?? data.createdAt ?? null,
            introOffer: !!data.introOffer,
          });
        });

        results.sort((a, b) => {
          try {
            return b.paidAt?.toDate() - a.paidAt?.toDate();
          } catch { return 0; }
        });

        setRecords(results);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(err);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
    load();
  }, []);

  function formatTs(ts: any): string {
    if (!ts) return '—';
    try { return format(ts.toDate(), 'MMM d, yyyy HH:mm'); } catch { return '—'; }
  }

  function copyToClipboard(text: string) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    setCopiedId(text);
    setTimeout(() => setCopiedId(null), 1500);
  }

  function exportCsv() {
    const header = ['User ID', 'Plan', 'Payment ID', 'Amount (INR)', 'Status', 'Intro Offer', 'Date'];
    const rows = filtered.map(r => [
      r.uid,
      r.planId,
      r.paymentId,
      r.amount,
      r.status,
      r.introOffer ? 'Yes' : 'No',
      formatTs(r.paidAt),
    ]);
    const csv = [header, ...rows].map(row => row.join(',')).join('\n');
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = `payment-history-${format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd')}.csv`;
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  }

  const filtered = planFilter === 'all'
    ? records
    : records.filter(r => r.planId === planFilter);

  const totalRevenue = filtered.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.amount, 0);
  const thisMonthRevenue = filtered.reduce((sum, r) => {
    try {
      return isAfter(r.paidAt.toDate(), startOfMonth(new Date())) ? sum + r.amount : sum;
    } catch { return sum; }
  }, 0);
  const paidCount = filtered.filter(r => r.amount > 0).length;
  const introCount = filtered.filter(r => r.introOffer).length;

  const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(filtered.length / PAGE_SIZE));
  const pageRecords = filtered.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_SIZE, page * PAGE_SIZE);

  const STAT_CARDS = [
    {
      label: 'Total Revenue',
      value: `₹${totalRevenue.toLocaleString('en-IN')}`,
      icon: IndianRupee,
      color: 'text-green-400',
      bg: 'bg-green-500/10',
    },
    {
      label: 'This Month',
      value: `₹${thisMonthRevenue.toLocaleString('en-IN')}`,
      icon: CalendarDays,
      color: 'text-indigo-400',
      bg: 'bg-indigo-500/10',
    },
    {
      label: 'Paid Subscriptions',
      value: paidCount,
      icon: Receipt,
      color: 'text-blue-400',
      bg: 'bg-blue-500/10',
    },
    {
      label: 'Intro Offer (₹0)',
      value: introCount,
      icon: TrendingUp,
      color: 'text-amber-400',
      bg: 'bg-amber-500/10',
    },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Payment History</h1>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">
            All subscriptions with a recorded payment ID
          </p>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={exportCsv}
          disabled={filtered.length === 0}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-700 hover:text-white disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
        >
          <Download className="h-4 w-4" />
          Export CSV
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Stats */}
      {loading ? (
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
          {Array.from({ length: 4 }).map((_, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="h-24 rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 animate-pulse" />
          ))}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
          {STAT_CARDS.map(card => (
            <div key={card.label} className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-5">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{card.label}</p>
                <div className={`rounded-lg p-2 ${card.bg}`}>
                  <card.icon className={`h-4 w-4 ${card.color}`} />
                </div>
              </div>
              <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{card.value}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Filter */}
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3 items-center">
        <select
          value={planFilter}
          onChange={e => { setPlanFilter(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
          className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
        >
          <option value="all">All Plans</option>
          <option value="free">Free</option>
          <option value="pro">Pro</option>
          <option value="enterprise">Enterprise</option>
        </select>
        <span className="text-sm text-slate-400 ml-auto">{filtered.length} payment records</span>
      </div>

      {loading ? (
        <SkeletonTable rows={10} cols={6} />
      ) : filtered.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 py-20 text-center">
          <Receipt className="h-10 w-10 text-slate-600 mx-auto mb-3" />
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm">No payment records found.</p>
          <p className="text-slate-500 text-xs mt-1">
            Records appear when a subscription has a <code className="text-slate-400">paymentId</code> set.
          </p>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <>
          <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="overflow-x-auto">
              <table className="w-full text-sm">
                <thead>
                  <tr className="bg-slate-800 border-b border-slate-700 sticky top-0">
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">User ID</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Plan</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Payment ID</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Amount</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Status</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Date</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/40">
                  {pageRecords.map((rec, i) => (
                    <tr
                      key={`${rec.uid}-${rec.paymentId}`}
                      className={`${i % 2 === 0 ? 'bg-slate-800' : 'bg-slate-800/50'} hover:bg-slate-700/40 transition-colors`}
                    >
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <span className="font-mono text-xs text-slate-300">{rec.uid.slice(0, 14)}…</span>
                          <button
                            onClick={() => copyToClipboard(rec.uid)}
                            className="text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 transition-colors"
                          >
                            {copiedId === rec.uid
                              ? <CheckCircle className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-400" />
                              : <Copy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <span className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium capitalize ${PLAN_COLORS[rec.planId] ?? PLAN_COLORS.free}`}>
                            {rec.planId}
                          </span>
                          {rec.introOffer && (
                            <span className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-amber-500/30 bg-amber-500/20 px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium text-amber-300">
                              Intro
                            </span>
                          )}
                        </div>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                          <span className="font-mono text-xs text-slate-300">
                            {rec.paymentId.length > 20
                              ? `${rec.paymentId.slice(0, 20)}…`
                              : rec.paymentId}
                          </span>
                          <button
                            onClick={() => copyToClipboard(rec.paymentId)}
                            className="text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 transition-colors"
                          >
                            {copiedId === rec.paymentId
                              ? <CheckCircle className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-400" />
                              : <Copy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <span className={`text-sm font-semibold ${rec.amount === 0 ? 'text-slate-400' : 'text-green-400'}`}>
                          {rec.amount === 0 ? '₹0' : `₹${rec.amount.toLocaleString('en-IN')}`}
                        </span>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <span className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium capitalize ${
                          rec.status === 'active' ? 'border-green-500/30 bg-green-500/15 text-green-300'
                          : rec.status === 'expired' ? 'border-red-500/30 bg-red-500/15 text-red-300'
                          : 'border-slate-600 bg-slate-700/50 text-slate-400'
                        }`}>
                          {rec.status}
                        </span>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400">{formatTs(rec.paidAt)}</td>
                    </tr>
                  ))}
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Pagination */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm text-slate-400">
            <span>{filtered.length} records • Page {page} of {totalPages}</span>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <button
                onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.max(1, p - 1))}
                disabled={page === 1}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
              >
                <ChevronLeft className="h-4 w-4" /> Prev
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.min(totalPages, p + 1))}
                disabled={page === totalPages}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
              >
                Next <ChevronRight className="h-4 w-4" />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { doc, getDoc, setDoc, Timestamp } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { format } from 'date-fns';
import {
  Loader2,
  Plus,
  Trash2,
  Eye,
  EyeOff,
  Smartphone,
  Building2,
  Banknote,
  Zap,
  Save,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { useToast } from '../components/Toast';

interface UpiEntry {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  upiId: string;
  isActive: boolean;
}

interface PaymentConfig {
  upi: {
    enabled: boolean;
    entries: UpiEntry[];
  };
  razorpay: {
    enabled: boolean;
    keyId: string;
    keySecret: string;
    webhookSecret: string;
  };
  bankTransfer: {
    enabled: boolean;
    accountName: string;
    accountNumber: string;
    ifscCode: string;
    bankName: string;
    branch: string;
  };
  cash: {
    enabled: boolean;
    instructions: string;
  };
  updatedAt?: any;
}

const DEFAULT_CONFIG: PaymentConfig = {
  upi: { enabled: false, entries: [] },
  razorpay: { enabled: false, keyId: '', keySecret: '', webhookSecret: '' },
  bankTransfer: {
    enabled: false,
    accountName: '',
    accountNumber: '',
    ifscCode: '',
    bankName: '',
    branch: '',
  },
  cash: { enabled: false, instructions: '' },
};

function Toggle({ value, onChange }: { value: boolean; onChange: (v: boolean) => void }) {
  return (
    <button
      type="button"
      onClick={() => onChange(!value)}
      className={`relative inline-flex h-6 w-11 items-center rounded-full transition-colors ${
        value ? 'bg-indigo-600' : 'bg-slate-600'
      }`}
    >
      <span
        className={`inline-block h-4 w-4 transform rounded-full bg-white transition-transform shadow-sm ${
          value ? 'translate-x-6' : 'translate-x-1'
        }`}
      />
    </button>
  );
}

function SectionCard({
  icon: Icon,
  title,
  description,
  enabled,
  onToggle,
  children,
}: {
  icon: any;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  enabled: boolean;
  onToggle: (v: boolean) => void;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  return (
    <div className={`rounded-xl border bg-slate-800 overflow-hidden transition-all ${
      enabled ? 'border-indigo-500/40' : 'border-slate-700'
    }`}>
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-4 border-b border-slate-700">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className={`flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center rounded-lg ${
            enabled ? 'bg-indigo-600' : 'bg-slate-700'
          }`}>
            <Icon className="h-4 w-4 text-white" />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-white">{title}</h3>
            <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{description}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <Toggle value={enabled} onChange={onToggle} />
      </div>
      {enabled && <div className="p-5">{children}</div>}
    </div>
  );
}

function MaskedInput({
  label,
  value,
  onChange,
  placeholder,
}: {
  label: string;
  value: string;
  onChange: (v: string) => void;
  placeholder?: string;
}) {
  const [show, setShow] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div>
      <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">{label}</label>
      <div className="relative">
        <input
          type={show ? 'text' : 'password'}
          value={value}
          onChange={e => onChange(e.target.value)}
          placeholder={placeholder}
          className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 pr-9 text-sm text-white font-mono placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
        />
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={() => setShow(v => !v)}
          className="absolute right-2.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-300"
        >
          {show ? <EyeOff className="h-4 w-4" /> : <Eye className="h-4 w-4" />}
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function PaymentsPage() {
  const { showToast } = useToast();
  const [config, setConfig] = useState<PaymentConfig>(DEFAULT_CONFIG);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      try {
        const snap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'config', 'payment_methods'));
        if (snap.exists()) {
          setConfig({ ...DEFAULT_CONFIG, ...(snap.data() as PaymentConfig) });
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(err);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
    load();
  }, []);

  async function handleSave() {
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      await setDoc(doc(db, 'config', 'payment_methods'), {
        ...config,
        updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
      });
      showToast('Payment settings saved', 'success');
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Failed to save', 'error');
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  function updateUpi(patch: Partial<PaymentConfig['upi']>) {
    setConfig(c => ({ ...c, upi: { ...c.upi, ...patch } }));
  }

  function addUpiEntry() {
    const entry: UpiEntry = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      label: '',
      upiId: '',
      isActive: true,
    };
    updateUpi({ entries: [...config.upi.entries, entry] });
  }

  function updateUpiEntry(id: string, patch: Partial<UpiEntry>) {
    updateUpi({
      entries: config.upi.entries.map(e => (e.id === id ? { ...e, ...patch } : e)),
    });
  }

  function removeUpiEntry(id: string) {
    updateUpi({ entries: config.upi.entries.filter(e => e.id !== id) });
  }

  function updateRazorpay(patch: Partial<PaymentConfig['razorpay']>) {
    setConfig(c => ({ ...c, razorpay: { ...c.razorpay, ...patch } }));
  }

  function updateBank(patch: Partial<PaymentConfig['bankTransfer']>) {
    setConfig(c => ({ ...c, bankTransfer: { ...c.bankTransfer, ...patch } }));
  }

  function updateCash(patch: Partial<PaymentConfig['cash']>) {
    setConfig(c => ({ ...c, cash: { ...c.cash, ...patch } }));
  }

  function formatTs(ts: any): string {
    if (!ts) return 'Never';
    try { return format(ts.toDate(), 'MMM d, yyyy HH:mm'); } catch { return '—'; }
  }

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-4 max-w-3xl">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Payment Methods</h1>
        {Array.from({ length: 4 }).map((_, i) => (
          <div key={i} className="h-20 rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 animate-pulse" />
        ))}
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6 max-w-3xl">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Payment Methods</h1>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">
            Configure how you receive subscription payments.
            Last saved: <span className="text-slate-300">{formatTs(config.updatedAt)}</span>
          </p>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={handleSave}
          disabled={saving}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 px-5 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-50 transition-colors"
        >
          {saving ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> : <Save className="h-4 w-4" />}
          Save All
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* UPI */}
      <SectionCard
        icon={Smartphone}
        title="UPI"
        description="Accept payments via Google Pay, PhonePe, Paytm, BHIM, and any UPI app"
        enabled={config.upi.enabled}
        onToggle={v => updateUpi({ enabled: v })}
      >
        <div className="space-y-3">
          {config.upi.entries.map((entry, i) => (
            <div key={entry.id} className="flex items-start gap-3 rounded-lg border border-slate-700 bg-slate-900 p-3">
              <div className="flex-1 grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1">Label</label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={entry.label}
                    onChange={e => updateUpiEntry(entry.id, { label: e.target.value })}
                    placeholder="e.g. Google Pay"
                    className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1">UPI ID</label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={entry.upiId}
                    onChange={e => updateUpiEntry(entry.id, { upiId: e.target.value })}
                    placeholder="yourname@upi"
                    className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm text-white font-mono placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
                  />
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 pt-5">
                <Toggle
                  value={entry.isActive}
                  onChange={v => updateUpiEntry(entry.id, { isActive: v })}
                />
                <button
                  onClick={() => removeUpiEntry(entry.id)}
                  className="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300 transition-colors"
                >
                  <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
          <button
            onClick={addUpiEntry}
            className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg border border-dashed border-slate-600 bg-slate-900/50 px-4 py-2.5 text-sm text-slate-400 hover:border-indigo-500 hover:text-indigo-300 transition-colors w-full justify-center"
          >
            <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
            Add UPI ID
          </button>
        </div>
      </SectionCard>

      {/* Razorpay */}
      <SectionCard
        icon={Zap}
        title="Razorpay"
        description="Automated payment collection with cards, netbanking, wallets, and UPI"
        enabled={config.razorpay.enabled}
        onToggle={v => updateRazorpay({ enabled: v })}
      >
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Key ID</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={config.razorpay.keyId}
              onChange={e => updateRazorpay({ keyId: e.target.value })}
              placeholder="rzp_live_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white font-mono placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>
          <MaskedInput
            label="Key Secret"
            value={config.razorpay.keySecret}
            onChange={v => updateRazorpay({ keySecret: v })}
            placeholder="••••••••••••••••••••••••"
          />
          <div className="sm:col-span-2">
            <MaskedInput
              label="Webhook Secret"
              value={config.razorpay.webhookSecret}
              onChange={v => updateRazorpay({ webhookSecret: v })}
              placeholder="Webhook secret from Razorpay dashboard"
            />
          </div>
        </div>
        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-3">
          Keys are stored in Firestore and used by your backend to verify payments. Never share Key Secret publicly.
        </p>
      </SectionCard>

      {/* Bank Transfer */}
      <SectionCard
        icon={Building2}
        title="Bank Transfer / NEFT"
        description="Manual bank transfer with account details shown to the user"
        enabled={config.bankTransfer.enabled}
        onToggle={v => updateBank({ enabled: v })}
      >
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Account Name</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={config.bankTransfer.accountName}
              onChange={e => updateBank({ accountName: e.target.value })}
              placeholder="e.g. Shopkeeper Technologies Pvt Ltd"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Account Number</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={config.bankTransfer.accountNumber}
              onChange={e => updateBank({ accountNumber: e.target.value })}
              placeholder="XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white font-mono placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">IFSC Code</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={config.bankTransfer.ifscCode}
              onChange={e => updateBank({ ifscCode: e.target.value.toUpperCase() })}
              placeholder="SBIN0001234"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white font-mono placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Bank Name</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={config.bankTransfer.bankName}
              onChange={e => updateBank({ bankName: e.target.value })}
              placeholder="State Bank of India"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>
          <div className="sm:col-span-2">
            <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Branch</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              value={config.bankTransfer.branch}
              onChange={e => updateBank({ branch: e.target.value })}
              placeholder="MG Road, Bangalore"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      </SectionCard>

      {/* Cash */}
      <SectionCard
        icon={Banknote}
        title="Cash / Offline"
        description="Accept cash payments offline with custom instructions for users"
        enabled={config.cash.enabled}
        onToggle={v => updateCash({ enabled: v })}
      >
        <div>
          <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Instructions shown to user</label>
          <textarea
            value={config.cash.instructions}
            onChange={e => updateCash({ instructions: e.target.value })}
            rows={3}
            placeholder="e.g. Visit our office at... or Contact our support team at..."
            className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500 resize-none"
          />
        </div>
      </SectionCard>

      {/* Active summary */}
      <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 px-5 py-4">
        <p className="text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-3 uppercase tracking-wider">Currently Active Methods</p>
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
          {config.upi.enabled && config.upi.entries.some(e => e.isActive) ? (
            <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-full border border-green-500/30 bg-green-500/15 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-green-300">
              <Smartphone className="h-3 w-3" /> UPI ({config.upi.entries.filter(e => e.isActive).length} ID{config.upi.entries.filter(e => e.isActive).length !== 1 ? 's' : ''})
            </span>
          ) : null}
          {config.razorpay.enabled && config.razorpay.keyId ? (
            <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-full border border-green-500/30 bg-green-500/15 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-green-300">
              <Zap className="h-3 w-3" /> Razorpay
            </span>
          ) : null}
          {config.bankTransfer.enabled && config.bankTransfer.accountNumber ? (
            <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-full border border-green-500/30 bg-green-500/15 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-green-300">
              <Building2 className="h-3 w-3" /> Bank Transfer
            </span>
          ) : null}
          {config.cash.enabled ? (
            <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-full border border-green-500/30 bg-green-500/15 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-green-300">
              <Banknote className="h-3 w-3" /> Cash
            </span>
          ) : null}
          {!config.upi.enabled && !config.razorpay.enabled && !config.bankTransfer.enabled && !config.cash.enabled && (
            <span className="text-sm text-slate-500 italic">No payment methods enabled yet</span>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: artifacts\admin-panel\src\pages\PlansPage.tsx
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { doc, getDoc, setDoc, Timestamp } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { Loader2, CheckCircle, X } from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { Plan, FEATURE_KEYS, ALL_FEATURE_KEYS } from '../types';
import { useToast } from '../components/Toast';

const PLAN_IDS = ['free', 'pro', 'enterprise'];

export default function PlansPage() {
  const { showToast } = useToast();
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState<Record<string, Plan>>({});
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState<Record<string, boolean>>({});

  async function loadPlans() {
    try {
      const results: Record<string, Plan> = {};
      await Promise.all(
        PLAN_IDS.map(async id => {
          const snap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'plans', id));
          if (snap.exists()) {
            results[id] = { id, ...(snap.data() as Omit<Plan, 'id'>) };
          } else {
            results[id] = {
              id,
              name: id.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + id.slice(1),
              price: id === 'free' ? 0 : id === 'pro' ? 299 : 999,
              currency: 'INR',
              durationDays: 30,
              features: id === 'free' ? ['basic', 'waste_tracking'] : ALL_FEATURE_KEYS,
              isActive: true,
              createdAt: null,
              updatedAt: null,
            };
          }
        })
      );
      setPlans(results);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  useEffect(() => { loadPlans(); }, []);

  function updatePlan(id: string, field: keyof Plan, value: any) {
    setPlans(prev => ({ ...prev, [id]: { ...prev[id], [field]: value } }));
  }

  function toggleFeature(planId: string, key: string) {
    const plan = plans[planId];
    const hasFeature = plan.features.includes(key);
    const newFeatures = hasFeature
      ? plan.features.filter(f => f !== key)
      : [...plan.features, key];
    updatePlan(planId, 'features', newFeatures);
  }

  async function savePlan(id: string) {
    setSaving(prev => ({ ...prev, [id]: true }));
    try {
      const plan = plans[id];
      await setDoc(doc(db, 'plans', id), {
        name: plan.name,
        price: plan.price,
        currency: plan.currency,
        durationDays: plan.durationDays,
        features: plan.features,
        isActive: plan.isActive,
        updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
        ...(plan.createdAt ? {} : { createdAt: Timestamp.now() }),
      }, { merge: true });
      showToast(`${plan.name} plan saved`, 'success');
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Failed to save plan', 'error');
    } finally {
      setSaving(prev => ({ ...prev, [id]: false }));
    }
  }

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="space-y-4">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Plans</h1>
        {Array.from({ length: 3 }).map((_, i) => (
          <div key={i} className="h-64 rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 animate-pulse" />
        ))}
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6 max-w-4xl">
      <div>
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Plans</h1>
        <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">Manage subscription plan configurations</p>
      </div>

      {PLAN_IDS.map(id => {
        const plan = plans[id];
        if (!plan) return null;
        return (
          <div key={id} className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-4 border-b border-slate-700">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <h2 className="text-base font-semibold text-white capitalize">{plan.name}</h2>
                <button
                  onClick={() => updatePlan(id, 'isActive', !plan.isActive)}
                  className={`relative inline-flex h-5 w-9 items-center rounded-full transition-colors ${
                    plan.isActive ? 'bg-indigo-600' : 'bg-slate-600'
                  }`}
                >
                  <span
                    className={`inline-block h-3.5 w-3.5 transform rounded-full bg-white transition-transform ${
                      plan.isActive ? 'translate-x-4.5' : 'translate-x-0.5'
                    }`}
                  />
                </button>
                <span className={`text-xs ${plan.isActive ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-slate-500'}`}>
                  {plan.isActive ? 'Active' : 'Inactive'}
                </span>
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={() => savePlan(id)}
                disabled={saving[id]}
                className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-50 transition-colors"
              >
                {saving[id] ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> : null}
                Save
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="p-5 space-y-5">
              {/* Basic fields */}
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Plan Name</label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={plan.name}
                    onChange={e => updatePlan(id, 'name', e.target.value)}
                    className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Price (INR)</label>
                  <input
                    type="number"
                    min={0}
                    value={plan.price}
                    onChange={e => updatePlan(id, 'price', Number(e.target.value))}
                    className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-1.5">Duration (days)</label>
                  <input
                    type="number"
                    min={1}
                    value={plan.durationDays}
                    onChange={e => updatePlan(id, 'durationDays', Number(e.target.value))}
                    className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
                  />
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Features */}
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs text-slate-400 mb-3">Features</label>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                  {ALL_FEATURE_KEYS.map(key => {
                    const included = plan.features.includes(key);
                    return (
                      <button
                        key={key}
                        onClick={() => toggleFeature(id, key)}
                        className={`flex items-center gap-3 rounded-lg border px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm text-left transition-all ${
                          included
                            ? 'border-indigo-500/50 bg-indigo-500/10 text-indigo-200'
                            : 'border-slate-700 bg-slate-800/60 text-slate-500 hover:border-slate-600 hover:text-slate-400'
                        }`}
                      >
                        {included
                          ? <CheckCircle className="h-4 w-4 text-indigo-400 shrink-0" />
                          : <X className="h-4 w-4 text-slate-600 shrink-0" />}
                        <span>{FEATURE_KEYS[key]}</span>
                      </button>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}

[END: artifacts\admin-panel\src\pages\PlansPage.tsx]

FILE: artifacts\admin-panel\src\pages\UserDetailPage.tsx
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useParams, Link } from 'react-router-dom';
import { doc, onSnapshot, collection, query, where, orderBy, getDocs } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { format } from 'date-fns';
import { ArrowLeft, Copy, CheckCircle, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { SubscriptionRecord, AuditLog } from '../types';
import {
  adminChangePlan,
  adminExtendSubscription,
  adminCancelSubscription,
} from '../services/adminService';
import StatusBadge from '../components/StatusBadge';
import ConfirmModal from '../components/ConfirmModal';
import { useToast } from '../components/Toast';

interface PendingAction {
  type: 'change_plan' | 'extend' | 'cancel';
  label: string;
  description: string;
  variant: 'simple' | 'destructive';
  color: 'red' | 'indigo';
}

export default function UserDetailPage() {
  const { uid } = useParams<{ uid: string }>();
  const { showToast } = useToast();

  const [subscription, setSubscription] = useState<SubscriptionRecord | null>(null);
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<AuditLog[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);

  const [selectedPlan, setSelectedPlan] = useState('free');
  const [extendDays, setExtendDays] = useState(30);
  const [actionLoading, setActionLoading] = useState(false);
  const [pendingAction, setPendingAction] = useState<PendingAction | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!uid) return;
    setLoading(true);

    // Real-time subscription updates
    const unsubSub = onSnapshot(
      doc(db, 'users', uid, 'subscription', 'current'),
      (snap) => {
        if (snap.exists()) {
          const data = snap.data() as SubscriptionRecord;
          setSubscription(data);
          setSelectedPlan(data.planId ?? data.plan ?? 'free');
        } else {
          setSubscription(null);
        }
      },
      (err) => console.error('Error loading subscription:', err)
    );

    // Real-time audit logs updates
    const unsubLogs = onSnapshot(
      query(
        collection(db, 'subscription_logs'),
        where('userId', '==', uid),
        orderBy('timestamp', 'desc')
      ),
      (snap) => {
        setLogs(snap.docs.map(d => ({ id: d.id, ...(d.data() as Omit<AuditLog, 'id'>) })));
        setLoading(false);
      },
      (err) => {
        console.error('Error loading audit logs:', err);
        setLoading(false);
      }
    );

    return () => {
      unsubSub();
      unsubLogs();
    };
  }, [uid]);

  function formatTs(ts: any): string {
    if (!ts) return '—';
    try { return format(ts.toDate(), 'MMM d, yyyy HH:mm'); } catch { return '—'; }
  }

  function copyUid() {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(uid ?? '');
    setCopied(true);
    setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 1500);
  }

  // Called after confirm modal approves
  async function executeAction() {
    if (!uid || !pendingAction) return;
    setActionLoading(true);
    try {
      if (pendingAction.type === 'change_plan') {
        await adminChangePlan(uid, selectedPlan);
        showToast(`Plan changed to ${selectedPlan}`, 'success');
      } else if (pendingAction.type === 'extend') {
        await adminExtendSubscription(uid, extendDays);
        showToast(`Subscription extended by ${extendDays} days`, 'success');
      } else if (pendingAction.type === 'cancel') {
        await adminCancelSubscription(uid);
        showToast('Subscription cancelled', 'success');
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Action failed', 'error');
    } finally {
      setActionLoading(false);
    }
  }

  const currentPlanLabel = subscription?.planId ?? subscription?.plan ?? 'free';

  const fields: [string, string][] = subscription
    ? [
        ['Plan ID', subscription.planId ?? subscription.plan ?? '—'],
        ['Status', subscription.status],
        ['Start Date', formatTs(subscription.startDate)],
        ['End Date', formatTs(subscription.endDate)],
        ['Grace End Date', formatTs(subscription.graceEndDate)],
        ['Trial Used', String(subscription.trialUsed ?? false)],
        ['Auto Renew', String(subscription.autoRenew ?? false)],
        ['Payment ID', subscription.paymentId ?? '—'],
        ['Source', subscription.source ?? '—'],
        ['Intro Offer', String(subscription.introOffer ?? false)],
        ['Created At', formatTs(subscription.createdAt)],
        ['Updated At', formatTs(subscription.updatedAt)],
      ]
    : [];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6 max-w-4xl">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <Link
          to="/users"
          className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-sm text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-colors"
        >
          <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" /> Back to Users
        </Link>
      </div>

      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">User Detail</h1>
      </div>

      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 px-4 py-3">
        <span className="text-xs text-slate-400 font-medium">UID:</span>
        <code className="text-sm text-slate-200 font-mono flex-1">{uid}</code>
        <button onClick={copyUid} className="text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-200">
          {copied ? <CheckCircle className="h-4 w-4 text-green-400" /> : <Copy className="h-4 w-4" />}
        </button>
      </div>

      {loading ? (
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {Array.from({ length: 3 }).map((_, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="h-24 rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 animate-pulse" />
          ))}
        </div>
      ) : !subscription ? (
        <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 py-12 text-center text-slate-500">
          No subscription found for this user.
        </div>
      ) : (
        <>
          {/* Subscription record */}
          <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="px-5 py-4 border-b border-slate-700 flex items-center justify-between">
              <h2 className="font-semibold text-white">Subscription Record</h2>
              <StatusBadge status={subscription.status} />
            </div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-0 divide-y sm:divide-y-0 divide-slate-700/50">
              {fields.map(([label, value], i) => (
                <div
                  key={label}
                  className={`px-5 py-3 ${i % 2 === 0 ? 'bg-slate-800' : 'bg-slate-800/60'} border-b border-slate-700/40 flex justify-between items-center`}
                >
                  <span className="text-xs text-slate-400">{label}</span>
                  <span className="text-sm text-slate-200 font-medium capitalize">{value}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Actions */}
          <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="px-5 py-4 border-b border-slate-700">
              <h2 className="font-semibold text-white">Subscription Actions</h2>
              <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-0.5">All actions require confirmation before applying</p>
            </div>
            <div className="p-5 space-y-5">
              {/* Change plan */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-wrap">
                <label className="text-sm text-slate-300 w-36 shrink-0">Change Plan</label>
                <select
                  value={selectedPlan}
                  onChange={e => setSelectedPlan(e.target.value)}
                  className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
                >
                  <option value="free">Free</option>
                  <option value="pro">Pro</option>
                  <option value="enterprise">Enterprise</option>
                </select>
                <button
                  disabled={actionLoading}
                  onClick={() => setPendingAction({
                    type: 'change_plan',
                    label: `Change plan to ${selectedPlan}`,
                    description: `This will change the user's current plan from "${currentPlanLabel}" to "${selectedPlan}" immediately. The subscription source will be marked as "admin".`,
                    variant: 'simple',
                    color: 'indigo',
                  })}
                  className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-50 transition-colors"
                >
                  {actionLoading && pendingAction?.type === 'change_plan' && <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />}
                  Apply
                </button>
              </div>

              {/* Extend */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-wrap">
                <label className="text-sm text-slate-300 w-36 shrink-0">Extend Subscription</label>
                <input
                  type="number"
                  min={1}
                  value={extendDays}
                  onChange={e => setExtendDays(Number(e.target.value))}
                  className="w-24 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
                />
                <span className="text-sm text-slate-400">days</span>
                <button
                  disabled={actionLoading || extendDays < 1}
                  onClick={() => setPendingAction({
                    type: 'extend',
                    label: `Extend by ${extendDays} day${extendDays !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`,
                    description: `This will extend the user's subscription by ${extendDays} day${extendDays !== 1 ? 's' : ''} from the current end date.`,
                    variant: 'simple',
                    color: 'indigo',
                  })}
                  className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-50 transition-colors"
                >
                  {actionLoading && pendingAction?.type === 'extend' && <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />}
                  Extend
                </button>
              </div>

              {/* Cancel */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-wrap">
                <label className="text-sm text-slate-300 w-36 shrink-0">Cancel Subscription</label>
                <button
                  onClick={() => setPendingAction({
                    type: 'cancel',
                    label: 'Cancel Subscription',
                    description: 'This will immediately expire the subscription and reset the plan to free. This cannot be undone. Type CONFIRM to proceed.',
                    variant: 'destructive',
                    color: 'red',
                  })}
                  className="rounded-lg bg-red-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-red-500 transition-colors"
                >
                  Cancel Subscription
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Audit history */}
          <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="px-5 py-4 border-b border-slate-700">
              <h2 className="font-semibold text-white">Audit History</h2>
              <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-0.5">{logs.length} events</p>
            </div>
            {logs.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="py-10 text-center text-sm text-slate-500">No audit history</div>
            ) : (
              <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                <table className="w-full text-sm">
                  <thead>
                    <tr className="border-b border-slate-700 bg-slate-800/80">
                      <th className="px-5 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase">Action</th>
                      <th className="px-5 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase">By</th>
                      <th className="px-5 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase">Timestamp</th>
                      <th className="px-5 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase">Change</th>
                    </tr>
                  </thead>
                  <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/40">
                    {logs.map((log, i) => (
                      <tr key={log.id} className={i % 2 === 0 ? 'bg-slate-800' : 'bg-slate-800/50'}>
                        <td className="px-5 py-3">
                          <span className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full bg-indigo-500/20 border border-indigo-500/30 px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium text-indigo-300 capitalize">
                            {log.action?.replace('_', ' ')}
                          </span>
                        </td>
                        <td className="px-5 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400 capitalize">{log.performedBy}</td>
                        <td className="px-5 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400">{formatTs(log.timestamp)}</td>
                        <td className="px-5 py-3 text-xs">
                          {log.previousState && (
                            <span className="text-slate-500">
                              {(log.previousState as any)?.status ?? (log.previousState as any)?.planId ?? ''}
                              {' → '}
                            </span>
                          )}
                          <span className="text-slate-300">
                            {(log.newState as any)?.status ?? (log.newState as any)?.planId ?? ''}
                          </span>
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    ))}
                  </tbody>
                </table>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </>
      )}

      <ConfirmModal
        isOpen={!!pendingAction}
        onClose={() => setPendingAction(null)}
        onConfirm={executeAction}
        title={pendingAction?.label ?? ''}
        description={pendingAction?.description}
        variant={pendingAction?.variant ?? 'simple'}
        confirmColor={pendingAction?.color ?? 'indigo'}
        confirmLabel={pendingAction?.variant === 'destructive' ? 'Confirm' : 'Yes, apply'}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

[END: artifacts\admin-panel\src\pages\UserDetailPage.tsx]
