import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { Link } from 'react-router-dom';
import { collection, collectionGroup, getDocs } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { format, addDays } from 'date-fns';
import {
  Search,
  Copy,
  CheckCircle,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronRight,
  Users,
  UserX,
  Gift,
  X,
  Loader2,
  CalendarDays,
  RotateCcw,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { UserWithSubscription, Plan } from '../types';
import StatusBadge from '../components/StatusBadge';
import SkeletonTable from '../components/SkeletonTable';
import ConfirmModal from '../components/ConfirmModal';
import { useToast } from '../components/Toast';
import { useAuth } from '../context/AuthContext';
import { adminGrantSubscription, adminResetTrial } from '../services/adminService';

const PAGE_SIZE = 25;
const MAX_GRANT_DAYS = 30;

interface RawUser {
  uid: string;
  email?: string;
  displayName?: string;
  createdAt?: any;
  trialUsed?: boolean;
}

// Badge shown when trialUsed === true — purple/indigo tint matching main app trial colour
function TrialUsedBadge() {
  return (
    <span
      className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium"
      style={{
        background: 'rgba(99,102,241,0.15)',
        borderColor: 'rgba(167,139,250,0.3)',
        color: '#a78bfa',
      }}
    >
      Trial Used
    </span>
  );
}

interface GrantModalProps {
  user: RawUser;
  plans: Plan[];
  adminEmail: string;
  onClose: () => void;
  onSuccess: (uid: string) => void;
}

function GrantModal({ user, plans, adminEmail, onClose, onSuccess }: GrantModalProps) {
  const activePlans = plans.filter(p => p.isActive && p.id !== 'free');
  const [planId, setPlanId] = useState(activePlans[0]?.id ?? plans[0]?.id ?? '');
  const [days, setDays] = useState(7);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const { showToast } = useToast();
  const overlayRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const selectedPlan = plans.find(p => p.id === planId);
  const endPreview = addDays(new Date(), days);

  async function handleGrant() {
    if (!planId) return;
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      await adminGrantSubscription(user.uid, planId, days, adminEmail);
      showToast(`Subscription granted to ${user.email ?? user.uid.slice(0, 10)}`, 'success');
      onSuccess(user.uid);
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Failed to grant subscription', 'error');
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div
      ref={overlayRef}
      className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm p-4"
      onClick={e => { if (e.target === overlayRef.current) onClose(); }}
    >
      <div className="w-full max-w-md rounded-2xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 shadow-2xl">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-4 border-b border-slate-700">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-indigo-600">
              <Gift className="h-4 w-4 text-white" />
            </div>
            <div>
              <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold text-white">Grant Subscription</h2>
              <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono truncate max-w-52">
                {user.email ?? user.uid}
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-colors">
            <X className="h-5 w-5" />
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Body */}
        <div className="p-5 space-y-5">
          {/* Plan selector */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 mb-2">Plan</label>
            {plans.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">No plans found. Create plans first.</p>
            ) : (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-2">
                {plans.filter(p => p.id !== 'free').map(plan => (
                  <button
                    key={plan.id}
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setPlanId(plan.id)}
                    className={`flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border px-4 py-3 text-left transition-colors ${
                      planId === plan.id
                        ? 'border-indigo-500 bg-indigo-500/10'
                        : 'border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 hover:border-slate-500'
                    }`}
                  >
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-sm font-medium text-white capitalize">{plan.name}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{plan.durationDays} day plan</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-right">
                      <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-indigo-300">
                        ₹{plan.price.toLocaleString('en-IN')}
                      </p>
                      {!plan.isActive && (
                        <span className="text-[10px] text-orange-400">Inactive</span>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Duration */}
          <div>
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
              <label className="text-xs font-medium text-slate-400">Duration</label>
              <span className="text-xs text-slate-500">Max {MAX_GRANT_DAYS} days</span>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <input
                type="range"
                min={1}
                max={MAX_GRANT_DAYS}
                value={days}
                onChange={e => setDays(Number(e.target.value))}
                className="flex-1 accent-indigo-500"
              />
              <div className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-900 px-2">
                <input
                  type="number"
                  min={1}
                  max={MAX_GRANT_DAYS}
                  value={days}
                  onChange={e => {
                    const v = Math.min(MAX_GRANT_DAYS, Math.max(1, Number(e.target.value)));
                    setDays(v);
                  }}
                  className="w-10 bg-transparent text-center text-sm font-semibold text-white focus:outline-none py-1.5"
                />
                <span className="text-xs text-slate-400">days</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            {/* Preview */}
            <div className="mt-3 flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg border border-slate-700 bg-slate-900 px-3 py-2.5">
              <CalendarDays className="h-4 w-4 text-slate-400 shrink-0" />
              <div className="text-xs text-slate-400">
                Active from <span className="text-white font-medium">today</span> until{' '}
                <span className="text-green-400 font-medium">{format(endPreview, 'MMM d, yyyy')}</span>
                {selectedPlan && (
                  <span className="text-slate-500"> · {selectedPlan.name}</span>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Footer */}
        <div className="flex gap-3 px-5 pb-5">
          <button
            onClick={onClose}
            className="flex-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-700 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-600 transition-colors"
          >
            Cancel
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={handleGrant}
            disabled={saving || !planId}
            className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-indigo-600 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
          >
            {saving ? <Loader2 className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin" /> : <Gift className="h-4 w-4" />}
            Grant {days}d Subscription
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function UsersPage() {
  const { adminUser } = useAuth();
  const [subUsers, setSubUsers] = useState<UserWithSubscription[]>([]);
  const [noSubUsers, setNoSubUsers] = useState<RawUser[]>([]);
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState<Plan[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [tab, setTab] = useState<'with' | 'without'>('with');
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [planFilter, setPlanFilter] = useState('all');
  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState('all');
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [copiedId, setCopiedId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [grantTarget, setGrantTarget] = useState<RawUser | null>(null);

  // trialUsed keyed by uid — populated for ALL users from the users collection
  const [trialUsedMap, setTrialUsedMap] = useState<Map<string, boolean>>(new Map());
  // Reset trial confirmation: stores the target user (uid + display label)
  const [resetTrialTarget, setResetTrialTarget] = useState<{ uid: string; label: string } | null>(null);
  const [resetting, setResetting] = useState(false);

  const { showToast } = useToast();

  async function loadData() {
    try {
      const [subResult, usersResult, plansResult] = await Promise.allSettled([
        getDocs(collectionGroup(db, 'subscription')),
        getDocs(collection(db, 'users')),
        getDocs(collection(db, 'plans')),
      ]);

      // Plans
      if (plansResult.status === 'fulfilled') {
        const planList: Plan[] = plansResult.value.docs.map(d => ({
          id: d.id,
          ...(d.data() as Omit<Plan, 'id'>),
        }));
        setPlans(planList);
      }

      // Build trialUsed + profile map from users collection
      const newTrialUsedMap = new Map<string, boolean>();
      const profileMap = new Map<string, { email?: string; displayName?: string; createdAt?: any; trialUsed?: boolean }>();
      if (usersResult.status === 'fulfilled') {
        usersResult.value.forEach(d => {
          const data = d.data();
          const trialUsed = data.trialUsed === true;
          newTrialUsedMap.set(d.id, trialUsed);
          profileMap.set(d.id, {
            email: data.email,
            displayName: data.displayName,
            createdAt: data.createdAt,
            trialUsed,
          });
        });
        setTrialUsedMap(newTrialUsedMap);
      } else {
        console.error('users collection denied:', usersResult.reason);
      }

      // Subscriptions (collectionGroup)
      const subUids = new Set<string>();
      if (subResult.status === 'fulfilled') {
        const withSub: UserWithSubscription[] = subResult.value.docs.map(d => {
          const pathParts = d.ref.path.split('/');
          const uid = pathParts[1];
          subUids.add(uid);
          return { uid, subscription: d.data() as any };
        });
        setSubUsers(withSub);
      } else {
        console.error('subscription collectionGroup denied:', subResult.reason);
      }

      // Users without subscription
      if (usersResult.status === 'fulfilled') {
        const withoutSub: RawUser[] = [];
        usersResult.value.forEach(d => {
          if (!subUids.has(d.id)) {
            const data = d.data();
            withoutSub.push({
              uid: d.id,
              email: data.email,
              displayName: data.displayName,
              createdAt: data.createdAt,
              trialUsed: data.trialUsed === true,
            });
          }
        });
        setNoSubUsers(withoutSub);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  useEffect(() => { loadData(); }, []);

  function copyToClipboard(text: string) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    setCopiedId(text);
    setTimeout(() => setCopiedId(null), 1500);
  }

  function formatDate(ts: any): string {
    if (!ts) return '—';
    try { return format(ts.toDate(), 'MMM d, yyyy'); } catch { return '—'; }
  }

  // After granting, reload fresh data
  async function handleGrantSuccess(_uid: string) {
    setGrantTarget(null);
    setLoading(true);
    await loadData();
  }

  // Execute the confirmed reset
  async function executeResetTrial() {
    if (!resetTrialTarget || !adminUser) return;
    setResetting(true);
    try {
      await adminResetTrial(resetTrialTarget.uid, adminUser.uid);
      // Optimistically update local state so badge disappears immediately
      setTrialUsedMap(prev => {
        const next = new Map(prev);
        next.set(resetTrialTarget.uid, false);
        return next;
      });
      setNoSubUsers(prev =>
        prev.map(u => u.uid === resetTrialTarget.uid ? { ...u, trialUsed: false } : u)
      );
      showToast(
        `Trial reset for ${resetTrialTarget.label}. They can now receive a free trial.`,
        'success'
      );
    } catch (err: any) {
      showToast(err?.message ?? 'Failed to reset trial', 'error');
    } finally {
      setResetting(false);
    }
  }

  // --- WITH SUBSCRIPTION filtering ---
  const filteredWith = subUsers.filter(u => {
    const matchSearch = !search ||
      u.uid.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase());
    const matchPlan = planFilter === 'all' ||
      (u.subscription.planId ?? u.subscription.plan) === planFilter;
    const matchStatus = statusFilter === 'all' ||
      u.subscription.status === statusFilter;
    return matchSearch && matchPlan && matchStatus;
  });

  // --- WITHOUT SUBSCRIPTION filtering ---
  const filteredWithout = noSubUsers.filter(u => {
    const matchSearch = !search ||
      u.uid.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) ||
      (u.email ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase());
    return matchSearch;
  });

  const activeList = tab === 'with' ? filteredWith : filteredWithout;
  const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(activeList.length / PAGE_SIZE));
  const pageItems = activeList.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_SIZE, page * PAGE_SIZE);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4 flex-wrap">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Users</h1>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mt-1">
            {subUsers.length} with subscription · {noSubUsers.length} without
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Tab toggle */}
      <div className="flex gap-1 rounded-xl border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 p-1 w-fit">
        <button
          onClick={() => { setTab('with'); setPage(1); }}
          className={`flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors ${
            tab === 'with'
              ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow-sm'
              : 'text-slate-400 hover:text-white'
          }`}
        >
          <Users className="h-4 w-4" />
          With Subscription
          <span className={`rounded-full px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-bold ${
            tab === 'with' ? 'bg-indigo-500 text-white' : 'bg-slate-700 text-slate-300'
          }`}>
            {subUsers.length}
          </span>
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={() => { setTab('without'); setPage(1); }}
          className={`flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition-colors ${
            tab === 'without'
              ? 'bg-slate-700 text-white shadow-sm'
              : 'text-slate-400 hover:text-white'
          }`}
        >
          <UserX className="h-4 w-4" />
          Without Subscription
          <span className={`rounded-full px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-bold ${
            tab === 'without' ? 'bg-slate-600 text-white' : 'bg-slate-700 text-slate-300'
          }`}>
            {noSubUsers.length}
          </span>
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Filters */}
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div className="relative flex-1 min-w-48">
          <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-4 w-4 text-slate-400" />
          <input
            type="text"
            value={search}
            onChange={e => { setSearch(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
            placeholder={tab === 'with' ? 'Search by user ID…' : 'Search by UID or email…'}
            className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 pl-9 pr-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder:text-slate-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
          />
        </div>
        {tab === 'with' && (
          <>
            <select
              value={planFilter}
              onChange={e => { setPlanFilter(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
              className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            >
              <option value="all">All Plans</option>
              <option value="free">Free</option>
              {plans.filter(p => p.id !== 'free').map(p => (
                <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>{p.name}</option>
              ))}
            </select>
            <select
              value={statusFilter}
              onChange={e => { setStatusFilter(e.target.value); setPage(1); }}
              className="rounded-lg border border-slate-600 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500"
            >
              <option value="all">All Statuses</option>
              <option value="active">Active</option>
              <option value="trial">Trial</option>
              <option value="expired">Expired</option>
              <option value="grace">Grace</option>
            </select>
          </>
        )}
      </div>

      {loading ? (
        <SkeletonTable rows={10} cols={tab === 'with' ? 7 : 5} />
      ) : (
        <>
          {/* ── WITH SUBSCRIPTION TABLE ── */}
          {tab === 'with' && (
            <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                <table className="w-full text-sm">
                  <thead>
                    <tr className="bg-slate-800 border-b border-slate-700 sticky top-0">
                      <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">User ID</th>
                      <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Plan</th>
                      <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Status</th>
                      <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">End Date</th>
                      <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Source</th>
                      <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Badges</th>
                      <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                    </tr>
                  </thead>
                  <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/40">
                    {pageItems.length === 0 ? (
                      <tr>
                        <td colSpan={7} className="py-12 text-center text-slate-500">No users found</td>
                      </tr>
                    ) : (pageItems as UserWithSubscription[]).map((u, i) => {
                      const hasTrialUsed = trialUsedMap.get(u.uid) === true;
                      return (
                        <tr key={u.uid} className={`${i % 2 === 0 ? 'bg-slate-800' : 'bg-slate-800/50'} hover:bg-slate-700/50 transition-colors`}>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3">
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                              <span className="font-mono text-xs text-slate-300">{u.uid.slice(0, 14)}…</span>
                              <button onClick={() => copyToClipboard(u.uid)} className="text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 transition-colors" title="Copy UID">
                                {copiedId === u.uid ? <CheckCircle className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-400" /> : <Copy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
                              </button>
                            </div>
                          </td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3">
                            <span className="capitalize text-slate-200 text-xs font-medium">
                              {u.subscription.planId ?? u.subscription.plan ?? '—'}
                            </span>
                          </td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3"><StatusBadge status={u.subscription.status} /></td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400">{formatDate(u.subscription.endDate)}</td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400 capitalize">{u.subscription.source ?? '—'}</td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3">
                            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                              {u.subscription.introOffer && (
                                <span className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full bg-yellow-500/20 border border-yellow-500/30 px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium text-yellow-300">Intro</span>
                              )}
                              {hasTrialUsed && <TrialUsedBadge />}
                            </div>
                          </td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3">
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                              <Link to={`/users/${u.uid}`} className="rounded-md bg-indigo-600 px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 transition-colors">
                                View
                              </Link>
                              {hasTrialUsed && (
                                <button
                                  onClick={() => setResetTrialTarget({ uid: u.uid, label: u.uid.slice(0, 10) + '…' })}
                                  title="Reset free trial"
                                  className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-md border border-violet-500/30 bg-violet-500/10 px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-violet-300 hover:bg-violet-500/20 transition-colors"
                                >
                                  <RotateCcw className="h-3 w-3" />
                                  Reset Trial
                                </button>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      );
                    })}
                  </tbody>
                </table>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* ── WITHOUT SUBSCRIPTION TABLE ── */}
          {tab === 'without' && (
            <div className="rounded-xl border border-slate-700 overflow-hidden">
              {noSubUsers.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="py-16 text-center">
                  <UserX className="h-10 w-10 text-slate-600 mx-auto mb-3" />
                  <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm font-medium">All users have subscriptions</p>
                  <p className="text-slate-500 text-xs mt-1">No users found without a subscription document.</p>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                  <table className="w-full text-sm">
                    <thead>
                      <tr className="bg-slate-800 border-b border-slate-700 sticky top-0">
                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">User ID</th>
                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Email</th>
                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Joined</th>
                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Badges</th>
                        <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-slate-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody className="divide-y divide-slate-700/40">
                      {pageItems.length === 0 ? (
                        <tr>
                          <td colSpan={5} className="py-12 text-center text-slate-500">No users match your search</td>
                        </tr>
                      ) : (pageItems as RawUser[]).map((u, i) => (
                        <tr key={u.uid} className={`${i % 2 === 0 ? 'bg-slate-800' : 'bg-slate-800/50'} hover:bg-slate-700/50 transition-colors`}>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3">
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                              <span className="font-mono text-xs text-slate-300">{u.uid.slice(0, 14)}…</span>
                              <button onClick={() => copyToClipboard(u.uid)} className="text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-300 transition-colors" title="Copy UID">
                                {copiedId === u.uid ? <CheckCircle className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-green-400" /> : <Copy className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
                              </button>
                            </div>
                          </td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-300">
                            {u.email ? (
                              <span>{u.email}</span>
                            ) : (
                              <span className="text-slate-500 italic">—</span>
                            )}
                          </td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3 text-xs text-slate-400">{formatDate(u.createdAt)}</td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3">
                            {u.trialUsed && <TrialUsedBadge />}
                          </td>
                          <td className="px-4 py-3">
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                              <button
                                onClick={() => setGrantTarget(u)}
                                className="flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-md bg-indigo-600 px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-white hover:bg-indigo-500 transition-colors"
                              >
                                <Gift className="h-3 w-3" />
                                Grant Sub
                              </button>
                              {u.trialUsed && (
                                <button
                                  onClick={() => setResetTrialTarget({
                                    uid: u.uid,
                                    label: u.email ?? u.displayName ?? u.uid.slice(0, 10) + '…',
                                  })}
                                  className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-md border border-violet-500/30 bg-violet-500/10 px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-violet-300 hover:bg-violet-500/20 transition-colors"
                                >
                                  <RotateCcw className="h-3 w-3" />
                                  Reset Trial
                                </button>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      ))}
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Pagination */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm text-slate-400">
            <span>{activeList.length} users • Page {page} of {totalPages}</span>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <button
                onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.max(1, p - 1))}
                disabled={page === 1}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-40 transition-colors"
              >
                <ChevronLeft className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Prev
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.min(totalPages, p + 1))}
                disabled={page === totalPages}
                className="flex items-center gap-1 rounded-lg border border-slate-700 bg-slate-800 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-slate-700 disabled:opacity-40 transition-colors"
              >
                Next <ChevronRight className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </>
      )}

      {/* Grant Subscription modal */}
      {grantTarget && (
        <GrantModal
          user={grantTarget}
          plans={plans}
          adminEmail={adminUser?.email ?? 'admin'}
          onClose={() => setGrantTarget(null)}
          onSuccess={handleGrantSuccess}
        />
      )}

      {/* Reset Trial confirmation */}
      <ConfirmModal
        isOpen={!!resetTrialTarget}
        onClose={() => setResetTrialTarget(null)}
        onConfirm={executeResetTrial}
        title={`Reset free trial for ${resetTrialTarget?.label ?? 'this user'}?`}
        description="This will allow this user to receive a free trial again the next time their subscription document is absent. Use this for support cases only."
        variant="simple"
        confirmColor="red"
        confirmLabel={resetting ? 'Resetting…' : 'Reset Trial'}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

import {
  doc,
  getDoc,
  setDoc,
  addDoc,
  collection,
  Timestamp,
} from 'firebase/firestore';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { SubscriptionRecord } from '../types';

export async function adminResetTrial(
  uid: string,
  performedByUid: string
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    await setDoc(doc(db, 'users', uid), { trialUsed: false }, { merge: true });
    await addDoc(collection(db, 'subscription_logs'), {
      userId: uid,
      action: 'admin_reset_trial',
      previousState: { trialUsed: true },
      newState: { trialUsed: false },
      performedBy: performedByUid,
      timestamp: Timestamp.now(),
    });
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('[AdminPanel][resetTrial]', err);
    throw err;
  }
}

export async function writeAuditLog(entry: {
  userId: string;
  action: string;
  previousState: Record<string, any> | null;
  newState: Record<string, any>;
  performedBy: 'system' | 'admin';
}): Promise<void> {
  await addDoc(collection(db, 'subscription_logs'), {
    ...entry,
    previousState: entry.previousState
      ? JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(entry.previousState))
      : null,
    newState: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(entry.newState)),
    timestamp: Timestamp.now(),
  });
}

export async function adminChangePlan(uid: string, planId: string): Promise<void> {
  const subRef = doc(db, 'users', uid, 'subscription', 'current');
  const snap = await getDoc(subRef);
  const prev = snap.exists() ? snap.data() : null;
  const prevPlanId = prev?.planId ?? 'free';

  let action: string;
  const planOrder: Record<string, number> = { free: 0, pro: 1, enterprise: 2 };
  const prevOrder = planOrder[prevPlanId] ?? 0;
  const newOrder = planOrder[planId] ?? 0;
  if (newOrder > prevOrder) action = 'admin_upgrade';
  else if (newOrder < prevOrder) action = 'admin_downgrade';
  else action = 'admin_override';

  const now = Timestamp.now();
  const updates: Partial<SubscriptionRecord> = {
    planId,
    plan: planId,
    status: 'active',
    source: 'admin',
    updatedAt: now,
  };

  await setDoc(subRef, updates, { merge: true });
  await writeAuditLog({
    userId: uid,
    action,
    previousState: prev,
    newState: { ...prev, ...updates },
    performedBy: 'admin',
  });
}

export async function adminExtendSubscription(uid: string, days: number): Promise<void> {
  const subRef = doc(db, 'users', uid, 'subscription', 'current');
  const snap = await getDoc(subRef);
  const prev = snap.exists() ? snap.data() : null;

  const configSnap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'config', 'global'));
  const gracePeriodDays: number = configSnap.exists()
    ? (configSnap.data().gracePeriodDays ?? 3)
    : 3;

  const now = new Date();
  let baseDate = now;
  if (prev?.endDate) {
    const existingEnd: Date = prev.endDate.toDate();
    if (existingEnd > now) baseDate = existingEnd;
  }

  const newEnd = new Date(baseDate);
  newEnd.setDate(newEnd.getDate() + days);
  const newGraceEnd = new Date(newEnd);
  newGraceEnd.setDate(newGraceEnd.getDate() + gracePeriodDays);

  const updates = {
    endDate: Timestamp.fromDate(newEnd),
    graceEndDate: Timestamp.fromDate(newGraceEnd),
    status: 'active' as const,
    source: 'admin' as const,
    updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
  };

  await setDoc(subRef, updates, { merge: true });
  await writeAuditLog({
    userId: uid,
    action: 'admin_extend',
    previousState: prev,
    newState: { ...prev, ...updates },
    performedBy: 'admin',
  });
}

export async function adminCancelSubscription(uid: string): Promise<void> {
  const subRef = doc(db, 'users', uid, 'subscription', 'current');
  const snap = await getDoc(subRef);
  const prev = snap.exists() ? snap.data() : null;

  const updates = {
    status: 'expired' as const,
    planId: 'free',
    plan: 'free',
    autoRenew: false,
    source: 'admin' as const,
    updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
  };

  await setDoc(subRef, updates, { merge: true });
  await writeAuditLog({
    userId: uid,
    action: 'admin_cancel',
    previousState: prev,
    newState: { ...prev, ...updates },
    performedBy: 'admin',
  });
}

export async function adminGrantSubscription(
  uid: string,
  planId: string,
  durationDays: number,
  adminEmail = 'admin'
): Promise<void> {
  const subRef = doc(db, 'users', uid, 'subscription', 'current');
  const now = Timestamp.now();
  const endDate = new Date();
  endDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() + durationDays);

  const configSnap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'config', 'global'));
  const gracePeriodDays: number = configSnap.exists()
    ? (configSnap.data().gracePeriodDays ?? 3)
    : 3;
  const graceEnd = new Date(endDate);
  graceEnd.setDate(graceEnd.getDate() + gracePeriodDays);

  const newSub: SubscriptionRecord = {
    planId,
    plan: planId,
    status: 'active',
    startDate: now,
    endDate: Timestamp.fromDate(endDate),
    graceEndDate: Timestamp.fromDate(graceEnd),
    trialUsed: false,
    autoRenew: false,
    paymentId: null,
    source: 'admin',
    createdAt: now,
    updatedAt: now,
  };

  await setDoc(subRef, newSub);
  await writeAuditLog({
    userId: uid,
    action: 'admin_grant',
    previousState: null,
    newState: { ...(newSub as unknown as Record<string, any>), adminEmail },
    performedBy: 'admin',
  });
}

export async function adminUpdateUserSubscription(
  uid: string,
  payload: Partial<SubscriptionRecord>
): Promise<void> {
  const subRef = doc(db, 'users', uid, 'subscription', 'current');
  const snap = await getDoc(subRef);
  const prev = snap.exists() ? snap.data() : null;

  const updates = {
    ...payload,
    source: 'admin' as const,
    updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
  };

  await setDoc(subRef, updates, { merge: true });
  await writeAuditLog({
    userId: uid,
    action: 'admin_override',
    previousState: prev,
    newState: { ...prev, ...updates },
    performedBy: 'admin',
  });
}

export interface SubscriptionRecord {
  planId: string;
  plan: string;
  status: 'active' | 'trial' | 'expired' | 'grace';
  startDate: any;
  endDate: any;
  graceEndDate: any;
  trialUsed: boolean;
  autoRenew: boolean;
  paymentId: string | null;
  source: 'system' | 'admin' | 'payment';
  introOffer?: boolean;
  createdAt: any;
  updatedAt: any;
}

export interface UserWithSubscription {
  uid: string;
  subscription: SubscriptionRecord;
}

export interface Plan {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  price: number;
  currency: 'INR';
  durationDays: number;
  features: string[];
  isActive: boolean;
  createdAt: any;
  updatedAt: any;
}

export interface GlobalConfig {
  freeTrialEnabled: boolean;
  trialDurationDays: number;
  defaultPlan: string;
  gracePeriodDays: number;
  appMode: 'free' | 'paid' | 'hybrid';
  updatedAt?: any;
}

export interface AuditLog {
  id: string;
  userId: string;
  action: string;
  previousState: Record<string, any> | null;
  newState: Record<string, any>;
  performedBy: 'system' | 'admin';
  timestamp: any;
}

export interface AdminUser {
  uid: string;
  email: string;
  role: 'super_admin' | 'support';
}

 * when building for iOS / Android, not for the Replit dev server.

import tailwindcss from '@tailwindcss/vite';
import path from 'path';

  base: '/',
  plugins: [react(), tailwindcss()],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, 'src'),
    },
    dedupe: ['react', 'react-dom'],
  },
  root: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname),
  build: {
    outDir: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, 'dist/cap'),
    emptyOutDir: true,
  },
});

import { defineConfig } from "vite";
import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react";
import tailwindcss from "@tailwindcss/vite";
import path from "path";
import runtimeErrorOverlay from "@replit/vite-plugin-runtime-error-modal";

const rawPort = process.env.PORT;

if (!rawPort) {
  throw new Error(
    "PORT environment variable is required but was not provided.",
  );
}

const port = Number(rawPort);

if (Number.isNaN(port) || port <= 0) {
  throw new Error(`Invalid PORT value: "${rawPort}"`);
}

const basePath = process.env.BASE_PATH;

if (!basePath) {
  throw new Error(
    "BASE_PATH environment variable is required but was not provided.",
  );
}

export default defineConfig({
  base: basePath,
  plugins: [
    react(),
    tailwindcss(),
    runtimeErrorOverlay(),
    ...(process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production" &&
    process.env.REPL_ID !== undefined
      ? [
          await import("@replit/vite-plugin-cartographer").then((m) =>
            m.cartographer({
              root: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, ".."),
            }),
          ),
          await import("@replit/vite-plugin-dev-banner").then((m) =>
            m.devBanner(),
          ),
        ]
      : []),
  ],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      "@": path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "src"),
      "@assets": path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "..", "..", "attached_assets"),
    },
    dedupe: ["react", "react-dom"],
  },
  root: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname),
  build: {
    outDir: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "dist/public"),
    emptyOutDir: true,
  },
  server: {
    port,
    strictPort: true,
    host: "0.0.0.0",
    allowedHosts: true,
    fs: {
      strict: true,
    },
  },
  preview: {
    port,
    host: "0.0.0.0",
    allowedHosts: true,
  },
});

import { createRequire } from "node:module";
import path from "node:path";
import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url";
import { build as esbuild } from "esbuild";
import esbuildPluginPino from "esbuild-plugin-pino";
import { rm } from "node:fs/promises";

// Plugins (e.g. 'esbuild-plugin-pino') may use `require` to resolve dependencies
globalThis.require = createRequire(import.meta.url);

const artifactDir = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));

async function buildAll() {
  const distDir = path.resolve(artifactDir, "dist");
  await rm(distDir, { recursive: true, force: true });

  await esbuild({
    entryPoints: [path.resolve(artifactDir, "src/index.ts")],
    platform: "node",
    bundle: true,
    format: "esm",
    outdir: distDir,
    outExtension: { ".js": ".mjs" },
    logLevel: "info",
    // Some packages may not be bundleable, so we externalize them, we can add more here as needed.
    // Some of the packages below may not be imported or installed, but we're adding them in case they are in the future.
    // Examples of unbundleable packages:
    // - uses native modules and loads them dynamically (e.g. sharp)
    // - use path traversal to read files (e.g. @google-cloud/secret-manager loads sibling .proto files)

import express, { type Express } from "express";
import cors from "cors";
import pinoHttp from "pino-http";
import router from "./routes";
import { logger } from "./lib/logger";

const app: Express = express();

app.use(
  pinoHttp({
    logger,
    serializers: {
      req(req) {
        return {
          id: req.id,
          method: req.method,
          url: req.url?.split("?")[0],
        };
      },
      res(res) {
        return {
          statusCode: res.statusCode,
        };
      },
    },
  }),
);
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

app.use("/api", router);

export default app;

import app from "./app";
import { logger } from "./lib/logger";

const rawPort = process.env["PORT"];

if (!rawPort) {
  throw new Error(
    "PORT environment variable is required but was not provided.",
  );
}

const port = Number(rawPort);

if (Number.isNaN(port) || port <= 0) {
  throw new Error(`Invalid PORT value: "${rawPort}"`);
}

app.listen(port, (err) => {
  if (err) {
    logger.error({ err }, "Error listening on port");
    process.exit(1);
  }

  logger.info({ port }, "Server listening");
});

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
FILE: lib\api-client-react\src\custom-fetch.ts
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export type CustomFetchOptions = RequestInit & {
  responseType?: "json" | "text" | "blob" | "auto";
};

export type ErrorType<T = unknown> = ApiError<T>;

export type BodyType<T> = T;

export type AuthTokenGetter = () => Promise<string | null> | string | null;

const NO_BODY_STATUS = new Set([204, 205, 304]);
const DEFAULT_JSON_ACCEPT = "application/json, application/problem+json";

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Module-level configuration
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

let _baseUrl: string | null = null;
let _authTokenGetter: AuthTokenGetter | null = null;

/**
 * Set a base URL that is prepended to every relative request URL
 * (i.e. paths that start with `/`).
 *
 * Useful for Expo bundles that need to call a remote API server.
 * Pass `null` to clear the base URL.
 */
export function setBaseUrl(url: string | null): void {
  _baseUrl = url ? url.replace(/\/+$/, "") : null;
}

/**
 * Register a getter that supplies a bearer auth token.  Before every fetch
 * the getter is invoked; when it returns a non-null string, an
 * `Authorization: Bearer <token>` header is attached to the request.
 *
 * Useful for Expo bundles making token-gated API calls.
 * Pass `null` to clear the getter.
 *
 * NOTE: This function should never be used in web applications where session
 * token cookies are automatically associated with API calls by the browser.
 */
export function setAuthTokenGetter(getter: AuthTokenGetter | null): void {
  _authTokenGetter = getter;
}

function isRequest(input: RequestInfo | URL): input is Request {
  return typeof Request !== "undefined" && input instanceof Request;
}

function resolveMethod(input: RequestInfo | URL, explicitMethod?: string): string {
  if (explicitMethod) return explicitMethod.toUpperCase();
  if (isRequest(input)) return input.method.toUpperCase();
  return "GET";
}

// Use loose check for URL — some runtimes (e.g. React Native) polyfill URL
// differently, so `instanceof URL` can fail.
function isUrl(input: RequestInfo | URL): input is URL {
  return typeof URL !== "undefined" && input instanceof URL;
}

function applyBaseUrl(input: RequestInfo | URL): RequestInfo | URL {
  if (!_baseUrl) return input;
  const url = resolveUrl(input);
  // Only prepend to relative paths (starting with /)
  if (!url.startsWith("/")) return input;

  const absolute = `${_baseUrl}${url}`;
  if (typeof input === "string") return absolute;
  if (isUrl(input)) return new URL(absolute);
  return new Request(absolute, input as Request);
}

function resolveUrl(input: RequestInfo | URL): string {
  if (typeof input === "string") return input;
  if (isUrl(input)) return input.toString();
  return input.url;
}

function mergeHeaders(...sources: Array<HeadersInit | undefined>): Headers {
  const headers = new Headers();

  for (const source of sources) {
    if (!source) continue;
    new Headers(source).forEach((value, key) => {
      headers.set(key, value);
    });
  }

  return headers;
}

function getMediaType(headers: Headers): string | null {
  const value = headers.get("content-type");
  return value ? value.split(";", 1)[0].trim().toLowerCase() : null;
}

function isJsonMediaType(mediaType: string | null): boolean {
  return mediaType === "application/json" || Boolean(mediaType?.endsWith("+json"));
}

function isTextMediaType(mediaType: string | null): boolean {
  return Boolean(
    mediaType &&
      (mediaType.startsWith("text/") ||
        mediaType === "application/xml" ||
        mediaType === "text/xml" ||
        mediaType.endsWith("+xml") ||
        mediaType === "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"),
  );
}

// Use strict equality: in browsers, `response.body` is `null` when the
// response genuinely has no content.  In React Native, `response.body` is
// always `undefined` because the ReadableStream API is not implemented —
// even when the response carries a full payload readable via `.text()` or
// `.json()`.  Loose equality (`== null`) matches both `null` and `undefined`,
// which causes every React Native response to be treated as empty.
function hasNoBody(response: Response, method: string): boolean {
  if (method === "HEAD") return true;
  if (NO_BODY_STATUS.has(response.status)) return true;
  if (response.headers.get("content-length") === "0") return true;
  if (response.body === null) return true;
  return false;
}

function stripBom(text: string): string {
  return text.charCodeAt(0) === 0xfeff ? text.slice(1) : text;
}

function looksLikeJson(text: string): boolean {
  const trimmed = text.trimStart();
  return trimmed.startsWith("{") || trimmed.startsWith("[");
}

function getStringField(value: unknown, key: string): string | undefined {
  if (!value || typeof value !== "object") return undefined;

  const candidate = (value as Record<string, unknown>)[key];
  if (typeof candidate !== "string") return undefined;

  const trimmed = candidate.trim();
  return trimmed === "" ? undefined : trimmed;
}

function truncate(text: string, maxLength = 300): string {
  return text.length > maxLength ? `${text.slice(0, maxLength - 1)}…` : text;
}

function buildErrorMessage(response: Response, data: unknown): string {
  const prefix = `HTTP ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`;

  if (typeof data === "string") {
    const text = data.trim();
    return text ? `${prefix}: ${truncate(text)}` : prefix;
  }

  const title = getStringField(data, "title");
  const detail = getStringField(data, "detail");
  const message =
    getStringField(data, "message") ??
    getStringField(data, "error_description") ??
    getStringField(data, "error");

  if (title && detail) return `${prefix}: ${title} — ${detail}`;
  if (detail) return `${prefix}: ${detail}`;
  if (message) return `${prefix}: ${message}`;
  if (title) return `${prefix}: ${title}`;

  return prefix;
}

export class ApiError<T = unknown> extends Error {
  readonly name = "ApiError";
  readonly status: number;
  readonly statusText: string;
  readonly data: T | null;
  readonly headers: Headers;
  readonly response: Response;
  readonly method: string;
  readonly url: string;

  constructor(
    response: Response,
    data: T | null,
    requestInfo: { method: string; url: string },
  ) {
    super(buildErrorMessage(response, data));
    Object.setPrototypeOf(this, new.target.prototype);

    this.status = response.status;
    this.statusText = response.statusText;
    this.data = data;
    this.headers = response.headers;
    this.response = response;
    this.method = requestInfo.method;
    this.url = response.url || requestInfo.url;
  }
}

export class ResponseParseError extends Error {
  readonly name = "ResponseParseError";
  readonly status: number;
  readonly statusText: string;
  readonly headers: Headers;
  readonly response: Response;
  readonly method: string;
  readonly url: string;
  readonly rawBody: string;
  readonly cause: unknown;

  constructor(
    response: Response,
    rawBody: string,
    cause: unknown,
    requestInfo: { method: string; url: string },
  ) {
    super(
      `Failed to parse response from ${requestInfo.method} ${response.url || requestInfo.url} ` +
        `(${response.status} ${response.statusText}) as JSON`,
    );
    Object.setPrototypeOf(this, new.target.prototype);

    this.status = response.status;
    this.statusText = response.statusText;
    this.headers = response.headers;
    this.response = response;
    this.method = requestInfo.method;
    this.url = response.url || requestInfo.url;
    this.rawBody = rawBody;
    this.cause = cause;
  }
}

async function parseJsonBody(
  response: Response,
  requestInfo: { method: string; url: string },
): Promise<unknown> {
  const raw = await response.text();
  const normalized = stripBom(raw);

  if (normalized.trim() === "") {
    return null;
  }

  try {
    return JSON.parse(normalized);
  } catch (cause) {
    throw new ResponseParseError(response, raw, cause, requestInfo);
  }
}

async function parseErrorBody(response: Response, method: string): Promise<unknown> {
  if (hasNoBody(response, method)) {
    return null;
  }

  const mediaType = getMediaType(response.headers);

  // Fall back to text when blob() is unavailable (e.g. some React Native builds).
  if (mediaType && !isJsonMediaType(mediaType) && !isTextMediaType(mediaType)) {
    return typeof response.blob === "function" ? response.blob() : response.text();
  }

  const raw = await response.text();
  const normalized = stripBom(raw);
  const trimmed = normalized.trim();

  if (trimmed === "") {
    return null;
  }

  if (isJsonMediaType(mediaType) || looksLikeJson(normalized)) {
    try {
      return JSON.parse(normalized);
    } catch {
      return raw;
    }
  }

  return raw;
}

function inferResponseType(response: Response): "json" | "text" | "blob" {
  const mediaType = getMediaType(response.headers);

  if (isJsonMediaType(mediaType)) return "json";
  if (isTextMediaType(mediaType) || mediaType == null) return "text";
  return "blob";
}

async function parseSuccessBody(
  response: Response,
  responseType: "json" | "text" | "blob" | "auto",
  requestInfo: { method: string; url: string },
): Promise<unknown> {
  if (hasNoBody(response, requestInfo.method)) {
    return null;
  }

  const effectiveType =
    responseType === "auto" ? inferResponseType(response) : responseType;

  switch (effectiveType) {
    case "json":
      return parseJsonBody(response, requestInfo);

    case "text": {
      const text = await response.text();
      return text === "" ? null : text;
    }

    case "blob":
      if (typeof response.blob !== "function") {
        throw new TypeError(
          "Blob responses are not supported in this runtime. " +
            "Use responseType \"json\" or \"text\" instead.",
        );
      }
      return response.blob();
  }
}

export async function customFetch<T = unknown>(
  input: RequestInfo | URL,
  options: CustomFetchOptions = {},
): Promise<T> {
  input = applyBaseUrl(input);
  const { responseType = "auto", headers: headersInit, ...init } = options;

  const method = resolveMethod(input, init.method);

  if (init.body != null && (method === "GET" || method === "HEAD")) {
    throw new TypeError(`customFetch: ${method} requests cannot have a body.`);
  }

  const headers = mergeHeaders(isRequest(input) ? input.headers : undefined, headersInit);

  if (
    typeof init.body === "string" &&
    !headers.has("content-type") &&
    looksLikeJson(init.body)
  ) {
    headers.set("content-type", "application/json");
  }

  if (responseType === "json" && !headers.has("accept")) {
    headers.set("accept", DEFAULT_JSON_ACCEPT);
  }

  // Attach bearer token when an auth getter is configured and no
  // Authorization header has been explicitly provided.
  if (_authTokenGetter && !headers.has("authorization")) {
    const token = await _authTokenGetter();
    if (token) {
      headers.set("authorization", `Bearer ${token}`);
    }
  }

  const requestInfo = { method, url: resolveUrl(input) };

  const response = await fetch(input, { ...init, method, headers });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const errorData = await parseErrorBody(response, method);
    throw new ApiError(response, errorData, requestInfo);
  }

  return (await parseSuccessBody(response, responseType, requestInfo)) as T;
}

/**
 * Generated by orval v8.5.3 🍺
 * Do not edit manually.
 * Api
 * API specification
 * OpenAPI spec version: 0.1.0
 */
import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import type {
  QueryFunction,
  QueryKey,
  UseQueryOptions,
  UseQueryResult,
} from "@tanstack/react-query";

import type { HealthStatus } from "./api.schemas";

import { customFetch } from "../custom-fetch";
import type { ErrorType } from "../custom-fetch";

type AwaitedInput<T> = PromiseLike<T> | T;

type Awaited<O> = O extends AwaitedInput<infer T> ? T : never;

type SecondParameter<T extends (...args: never) => unknown> = Parameters<T>[1];

/**
 * Returns server health status
 * @summary Health check
 */
export const getHealthCheckUrl = () => {
  return `/api/healthz`;
};

export const healthCheck = async (
  options?: RequestInit,
): Promise<HealthStatus> => {
  return customFetch<HealthStatus>(getHealthCheckUrl(), {
    ...options,
    method: "GET",
  });
};

export const getHealthCheckQueryKey = () => {
  return [`/api/healthz`] as const;
};

export const getHealthCheckQueryOptions = <
  TData = Awaited<ReturnType<typeof healthCheck>>,
  TError = ErrorType<unknown>,
>(options?: {
  query?: UseQueryOptions<
    Awaited<ReturnType<typeof healthCheck>>,
    TError,
    TData
  >;
  request?: SecondParameter<typeof customFetch>;
}) => {
  const { query: queryOptions, request: requestOptions } = options ?? {};

  const queryKey = queryOptions?.queryKey ?? getHealthCheckQueryKey();

  const queryFn: QueryFunction<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof healthCheck>>> = ({
    signal,
  }) => healthCheck({ signal, ...requestOptions });

  return { queryKey, queryFn, ...queryOptions } as UseQueryOptions<
    Awaited<ReturnType<typeof healthCheck>>,
    TError,
    TData
  > & { queryKey: QueryKey };
};

export type HealthCheckQueryResult = NonNullable<
  Awaited<ReturnType<typeof healthCheck>>
>;
export type HealthCheckQueryError = ErrorType<unknown>;

/**
 * @summary Health check
 */

export function useHealthCheck<
  TData = Awaited<ReturnType<typeof healthCheck>>,
  TError = ErrorType<unknown>,
>(options?: {
  query?: UseQueryOptions<
    Awaited<ReturnType<typeof healthCheck>>,
    TError,
    TData
  >;
  request?: SecondParameter<typeof customFetch>;
}): UseQueryResult<TData, TError> & { queryKey: QueryKey } {
  const queryOptions = getHealthCheckQueryOptions(options);

  const query = useQuery(queryOptions) as UseQueryResult<TData, TError> & {
    queryKey: QueryKey;
  };

  return { ...query, queryKey: queryOptions.queryKey };
}

import { defineConfig, InputTransformerFn } from "orval";
import path from "path";

const root = path.resolve(__dirname, "..", "..");
const apiClientReactSrc = path.resolve(root, "lib", "api-client-react", "src");
const apiZodSrc = path.resolve(root, "lib", "api-zod", "src");

// Our exports make assumptions about the title of the API being "Api" (i.e. generated output is `api.ts`).
const titleTransformer: InputTransformerFn = (config) => {
  config.info ??= {};
  config.info.title = "Api";

  return config;
};

export default defineConfig({
  "api-client-react": {
    input: {
      target: "./openapi.yaml",
      override: {
        transformer: titleTransformer,
      },
    },
    output: {
      workspace: apiClientReactSrc,
      target: "generated",
      client: "react-query",
      mode: "split",
      baseUrl: "/api",
      clean: true,
      prettier: true,
      override: {
        fetch: {
          includeHttpResponseReturnType: false,
        },
        mutator: {
          path: path.resolve(apiClientReactSrc, "custom-fetch.ts"),
          name: "customFetch",
        },
      },
    },
  },
  zod: {
    input: {
      target: "./openapi.yaml",
      override: {
        transformer: titleTransformer,
      },
    },
    output: {
      workspace: apiZodSrc,
      client: "zod",
      target: "generated",
      schemas: { path: "generated/types", type: "typescript" },
      mode: "split",
      clean: true,
      prettier: true,
      override: {
        zod: {
          coerce: {
            query: ['boolean', 'number', 'string'],
            param: ['boolean', 'number', 'string'],
            body: ['bigint', 'date'],
            response: ['bigint', 'date'],
          },
        },
        useDates: true,
        useBigInt: true,
      },
    },
  },
});

[END: lib\api-spec\orval.config.ts]
