────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
FILE: tools\set-admin-claim.cjs
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
/**
 * Set the superAdmin custom claim on a Firebase Auth user.
 *
 * Requirements:
 *   1. Node.js 18+ installed locally
 *   2. A service account JSON downloaded from Firebase Console:
 *        Project Settings → Service Accounts → Generate new private key
 *      Save it as  tools/service-account.json  (never commit this file)
 *
 * Usage:
 *   node tools/set-admin-claim.cjs <firebase-uid>
 *
 * Example:
 *   node tools/set-admin-claim.cjs 1WISSp0AKqVEDQ28YS1ZJGNNQxB3
 */

const path = require('path');
const fs   = require('fs');

// ── Check args ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const uid = process.argv[2];
if (!uid) {
  console.error('❌  Usage: node tools/set-admin-claim.cjs <firebase-uid>');
  process.exit(1);
}

// ── Check service account ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const saPath = path.resolve(__dirname, 'service-account.json');
if (!fs.existsSync(saPath)) {
  console.error('❌  Service account not found at: tools/service-account.json');
  console.error('');
  console.error('    Download it from Firebase Console:');
  console.error('    Project Settings → Service Accounts → Generate new private key');
  console.error('    Save as tools/service-account.json (it is gitignored)');
  process.exit(1);
}

// ── Load firebase-admin ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
let admin;
try {
  admin = require('firebase-admin');
} catch {
  console.error('❌  firebase-admin is not installed.');
  console.error('    Run:  cd tools && npm install');
  process.exit(1);
}

// ── Run ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const serviceAccount = require(saPath);

admin.initializeApp({
  credential: admin.credential.cert(serviceAccount),
});

console.log(`⏳  Setting superAdmin claim on UID: ${uid} …`);

admin.auth()
  .setCustomUserClaims(uid, { superAdmin: true })
  .then(() => {
    console.log('✅  Done! superAdmin: true claim set.');
    console.log('');
    console.log('    The user must sign out and sign back in for the claim to take effect.');
    process.exit(0);
  })
  .catch(err => {
    console.error('❌  Failed:', err.message);
    process.exit(1);
  });

[END: tools\set-admin-claim.cjs]


────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
FILE: docs\SHOPKEEPER_APP_DEVELOPER_REFERENCE.md
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# Shopkeeper App — Developer Reference

> **Audience:** The developer agent building the main Shopkeeper mobile/web app.
> **Source of truth:** This document is compiled directly from the Super Admin Panel source code (`artifacts/admin-panel/src/`). Every collection path, field name, enum value, and business rule described here is exactly what the admin panel reads and writes. Build the main app against these contracts without deviation.

---

## Table of Contents

1. [Firebase Project](#1-firebase-project)
2. [Authentication Architecture](#2-authentication-architecture)
3. [Firestore — Collection Reference](#3-firestore--collection-reference)
   - 3.1 `users/{uid}`
   - 3.2 `users/{uid}/subscription/current`
   - 3.3 `plans/{planId}`
   - 3.4 `config/global`
   - 3.5 `config/payment_methods`
   - 3.6 `subscription_logs/{autoId}`
   - 3.7 `announcements/{autoId}`
   - 3.8 `admins/{uid}`
4. [Subscription State Machine](#4-subscription-state-machine)
5. [Plan Hierarchy & Feature Keys](#5-plan-hierarchy--feature-keys)
6. [Admin Action Contracts](#6-admin-action-contracts)
7. [Payment Record Discovery](#7-payment-record-discovery)
8. [Giveaway / Grant Log](#8-giveaway--grant-log)
9. [Firestore Security Model](#9-firestore-security-model)
10. [Audit Log Reference](#10-audit-log-reference)
11. [Key Business Rules](#11-key-business-rules)

---

## 1. Firebase Project

| Property | Value |
|---|---|
| **Project ID** | `shopkeeper-1a3fc` |
| **Auth domain** | `shopkeeper-1a3fc.firebaseapp.com` |
| **Storage bucket** | `shopkeeper-1a3fc.appspot.com` |
| **SDK** | Firebase JS v10 (modular) |

The admin panel initialises Firebase with:

```ts
import { initializeApp } from 'firebase/app';
import { getFirestore } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { getAuth, GoogleAuthProvider } from 'firebase/auth';

const app = initializeApp({
  apiKey: "...",
  authDomain: "shopkeeper-1a3fc.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId: "shopkeeper-1a3fc",
  storageBucket: "shopkeeper-1a3fc.appspot.com",
  messagingSenderId: "...",
  appId: "...",
});

export const db   = getFirestore(app);
export const auth = getAuth(app);
export const googleProvider = new GoogleAuthProvider();
```

Use the exact same `projectId` / `authDomain` in the main app.

---

## 2. Authentication Architecture

### 2.1 Admin-panel auth (for context only — do NOT replicate in the main app)

The admin panel uses **Firebase Custom Claims** rather than a Firestore `admins` lookup:

```
signInWithEmailAndPassword / signInWithPopup
  → getIdTokenResult(forceRefresh = true)
    → token.claims.superAdmin === true  ✓ allow
    → anything else                    → firebaseSignOut() immediately
```

The `admins/{uid}` Firestore collection has **no client-readable security rule**, so the admin panel never reads it from the client. The custom claim is set via the Admin SDK:

```js
admin.auth().setCustomUserClaims(uid, { superAdmin: true });
```

### 2.2 Main-app auth (what you must implement)

Regular users sign in with `signInWithEmailAndPassword` or Google OAuth. They do **not** have `superAdmin: true` in their token. The main app must:

1. Call `onAuthStateChanged` to track the current user.
2. Read `users/{uid}` to get the user profile.
3. Read `users/{uid}/subscription/current` to get subscription state.
4. Gate features by checking `subscription.status` and `subscription.planId`.
5. **Never** write to `admins/`, `config/`, or `plans/` — those are admin-only.

---

## 3. Firestore — Collection Reference

### 3.1 `users/{uid}`

One document per Firebase Auth user. Created at registration.

```ts
interface UserDoc {
  email:       string;          // mirrors Auth email
  displayName: string;          // mirrors Auth displayName
  createdAt:   Timestamp;       // when the account was created
  trialUsed:   boolean;         // true once the user has consumed a free trial
}
```

**Important notes:**
- `trialUsed` starts as `false`. The main app sets it to `true` the moment a trial subscription is activated.
- The admin panel can reset `trialUsed` to `false` via `adminResetTrial()`. When this happens a `subscription_logs` entry is written with `action: 'admin_reset_trial'`.
- No other fields are written by the admin panel. The main app may add additional fields but must not remove or rename these four.

---

### 3.2 `users/{uid}/subscription/current`

A **single fixed-name document** (not auto-ID) at the sub-collection path `subscription/current`.

```ts
interface SubscriptionRecord {
  planId:       string;                            // 'free' | 'pro' | 'enterprise'
  plan:         string;                            // DUPLICATE of planId — always kept in sync
  status:       'active' | 'trial' | 'expired' | 'grace';
  startDate:    Timestamp;                         // when this period started
  endDate:      Timestamp;                         // when the paid/trial period ends
  graceEndDate: Timestamp;                         // endDate + gracePeriodDays (from config/global)
  trialUsed:    boolean;                           // whether this record represents a trial
  autoRenew:    boolean;                           // whether Razorpay auto-renew is active
  paymentId:    string | null;                     // Razorpay payment/order ID, null for admin grants
  source:       'system' | 'admin' | 'payment';   // how this sub was created/last modified
  introOffer?:  boolean;                           // optional: true if subscriber paid ₹0 intro price
  createdAt:    Timestamp;
  updatedAt:    Timestamp;
}
```

**Reading this document** — collectionGroup query used by admin panel:

```ts
getDocs(collectionGroup(db, 'subscription'))
// path of each doc: users/{uid}/subscription/current
// extract uid from: d.ref.path.split('/')[1]
```

**The main app reads this document** by direct reference:

```ts
const subRef = doc(db, 'users', uid, 'subscription', 'current');
const snap = await getDoc(subRef);
```

**Field duplication:** Both `planId` and `plan` always hold the same value (e.g. `'pro'`). Write both when you write either. This duplication exists for legacy reasons — older reads used `plan`, newer code uses `planId`. Support reading whichever is present:

```ts
const planId = data.planId ?? data.plan ?? 'free';
```

---

### 3.3 `plans/{planId}`

Three documents, with fixed IDs: **`free`**, **`pro`**, **`enterprise`**.

```ts
interface Plan {
  id:          string;    // document ID — 'free' | 'pro' | 'enterprise'
  name:        string;    // human-readable, e.g. "Pro Plan"
  price:       number;    // amount in INR (integer), e.g. 499
  currency:    'INR';     // always INR
  durationDays: number;   // subscription length, e.g. 30 or 365
  features:    string[];  // array of FEATURE_KEYS (see §5)
  isActive:    boolean;   // if false, don't offer this plan to new users
  createdAt:   Timestamp;
  updatedAt:   Timestamp;
}
```

**Example `pro` document:**

```json
{
  "name": "Pro Plan",
  "price": 499,
  "currency": "INR",
  "durationDays": 30,
  "features": ["basic", "waste_tracking", "analytics", "reports", "pos_billing"],
  "isActive": true
}
```

The admin panel allows editing all fields. The main app should:
- Fetch `plans/` collection to display plan pricing.
- Derive what features are enabled for the current user from `plans/{subscription.planId}.features`.
- Check `plan.isActive` before rendering a plan as purchasable.

**Plan hierarchy (for upgrade/downgrade logic):**

```
free (0) < pro (1) < enterprise (2)
```

This order is used by `adminChangePlan()` to determine audit action: `'upgrade'`, `'downgrade'`, or `'admin_override'`.

---

### 3.4 `config/global`

A **single document** at path `config/global`. Contains app-wide settings.

```ts
interface GlobalConfig {
  freeTrialEnabled:  boolean;           // whether new users can start a free trial
  trialDurationDays: number;            // how many days a trial lasts, e.g. 7
  defaultPlan:       string;            // planId to assign on signup, usually 'free'
  gracePeriodDays:   number;            // days after endDate before status → 'expired', e.g. 3
  appMode:           'free' | 'paid' | 'hybrid';
  updatedAt?:        Timestamp;
}
```

**`appMode` meanings:**

| Value | Meaning |
|---|---|
| `'free'` | All features are free; subscriptions are not enforced |
| `'paid'` | Full paywall; users must subscribe |
| `'hybrid'` | Free tier exists; premium features require subscription |

The main app must read this document at startup (or subscribe with `onSnapshot`) and adapt its feature-gating logic accordingly. Cache it locally — it changes rarely.

**Grace period logic** (implemented by admin panel and expected of main app):

```
if (now > endDate && now <= graceEndDate) → status = 'grace'
if (now > graceEndDate)                  → status = 'expired'
```

The `graceEndDate` is pre-computed as `endDate + gracePeriodDays` and stored on the subscription document, so the main app can compare dates without reading `config/global` on every check.

---

### 3.5 `config/payment_methods`

A **single document** at path `config/payment_methods`. Contains all payment configuration. The main app reads this to know which payment options to show.

```ts
interface PaymentConfig {
  upi: {
    enabled: boolean;
    entries: Array<{
      id:       string;   // unique key, e.g. 'upi_1'
      label:    string;   // display name, e.g. 'Shopkeeper Official'
      upiId:    string;   // e.g. 'shopkeeper@upi'
      isActive: boolean;  // only show entries where isActive === true
    }>;
  };
  razorpay: {
    enabled:       boolean;
    keyId:         string;  // Razorpay Key ID (starts with 'rzp_')
    keySecret:     string;  // ⚠️ DO NOT expose to client — read from backend only
    webhookSecret: string;  // ⚠️ DO NOT expose to client
  };
  bankTransfer: {
    enabled:       boolean;
    accountName:   string;
    accountNumber: string;
    ifscCode:      string;
    bankName:      string;
    branch:        string;
  };
  cash: {
    enabled:      boolean;
    instructions: string;  // free-text instructions for cash payment
  };
  updatedAt: Timestamp;
}
```

> **Security note:** `razorpay.keySecret` and `razorpay.webhookSecret` are stored in this document by the admin panel. The main app must **never** read these fields on the client. Only use `razorpay.keyId` on the client. The secret and webhook values are for a backend/Cloud Function only.

---

### 3.6 `subscription_logs/{autoId}`

Auto-ID collection. Every subscription mutation (by admin or by the system) writes one document here. This is the primary audit trail.

```ts
interface AuditLog {
  id:             string;                    // document ID (auto-generated)
  userId:         string;                    // uid of the affected user
  action:         string;                    // see §10 for all action values
  previousState:  Record<string, any> | null; // snapshot before the change, null for first grant
  newState:       Record<string, any>;        // snapshot after the change
  performedBy:    'system' | 'admin';        // 'admin' = human; 'system' = automated
  timestamp:      Timestamp;
}
```

The main app **should write** to this collection whenever it modifies a subscription (e.g. when a user starts a trial, completes a payment, or the system detects expiry). Use `performedBy: 'system'` for automated changes.

---

### 3.7 `announcements/{autoId}`

Auto-ID collection. Admin-authored messages displayed in the main app.

```ts
interface Announcement {
  id:             string;    // document ID
  title:          string;    // short headline
  message:        string;    // body text (may contain line breaks)
  type:           'info' | 'warning' | 'success' | 'maintenance';
  isActive:       boolean;   // only show to users when true
  targetAudience: 'all' | 'active' | 'expired';
  createdAt:      Timestamp;
  createdBy:      string;    // admin UID
  expiresAt:      Timestamp | null;  // if set, stop showing after this date
}
```

**Main app display logic:**

```ts
// Fetch active, non-expired announcements for the current user
const now = Timestamp.now();
query(
  collection(db, 'announcements'),
  where('isActive', '==', true),
  orderBy('createdAt', 'desc')
)
// Then filter client-side:
//   if (expiresAt && now > expiresAt)  → skip
//   if (targetAudience === 'active')   → show only to users with status 'active'
//   if (targetAudience === 'expired')  → show only to users with status 'expired'
//   if (targetAudience === 'all')      → show to everyone
```

**`type` → UI treatment:**

| Type | Colour / Icon |
|---|---|
| `info` | Blue / info icon |
| `warning` | Amber / warning triangle |
| `success` | Green / check circle |
| `maintenance` | Orange / wrench / may need to block app usage |

---

### 3.8 `admins/{uid}`

Documents for admin-panel users only. The main app must **never read or write** this collection. Firestore rules do not grant client read access to it.

```ts
interface AdminDoc {
  email:     string;
  role:      'super_admin' | 'support';
  createdAt: Timestamp;
}
```

---

## 4. Subscription State Machine

```
              ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
              │              New user signs up               │
              └──────────────────────┬──────────────────────┘
                                     │
                    freeTrialEnabled? │
                   ┌─────────────────┴────────────────┐
                   │ yes                               │ no
                   ▼                                   ▼
             status='trial'                    status='expired'
             planId=defaultPlan               planId='free'
             endDate=now+trialDays
                   │
          endDate reached?
                   │
                   ▼
             status='grace'   ◄── graceEndDate not yet passed
                   │
          graceEndDate reached?
                   │
                   ▼
             status='expired'
                   │
      user pays / admin grants
                   │
                   ▼
             status='active'
             planId='pro'|'enterprise'
             source='payment'|'admin'
                   │
          endDate reached?  (repeat grace→expired cycle)
```

**Status definitions:**

| Status | Access level |
|---|---|
| `'active'` | Full access to all features in their plan |
| `'trial'` | Access to features of the `defaultPlan` for the trial duration |
| `'grace'` | Plan features still accessible; show "renew soon" warning |
| `'expired'` | Downgrade to free tier or block, depending on `appMode` |

---

## 5. Plan Hierarchy & Feature Keys

### 5.1 Plan order

```
free (0) → pro (1) → enterprise (2)
```

### 5.2 Feature keys

These are the canonical string values used in `plan.features[]`. The main app gates UI sections using these exact strings.

```ts
const FEATURE_KEYS = {
  basic:               'Core Billing',
  waste_tracking:      'Waste Log',
  analytics:           'Sales & Purchase Dashboards',
  advanced_analytics:  'Advanced Analytics',
  reports:             'GST Reports',
  pos_billing:         'POS Quick Billing',
  bulk_import:         'Bulk CSV Import',
  stock_valuation:     'Stock Valuation',
  game_timeline:       'Activity Timeline',
  whatsapp_reminders:  'WhatsApp Reminders',
  multi_user:          'Staff Accounts',
  daily_snapshot:      'Daily Snapshots',
};
```

**Feature gate pattern (main app):**

```ts
// 1. Fetch plan once and cache
const planSnap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'plans', subscription.planId));
const enabledFeatures: string[] = planSnap.data()?.features ?? [];

// 2. Check before rendering a feature
function canAccess(featureKey: string): boolean {
  if (globalConfig.appMode === 'free') return true;
  if (subscription.status === 'expired' && globalConfig.appMode === 'paid') return false;
  return enabledFeatures.includes(featureKey);
}

// 3. Example usage
if (canAccess('pos_billing')) { /* show POS screen */ }
```

---

## 6. Admin Action Contracts

These are the exact operations the admin panel performs. The main app may need to mirror some (e.g. trial activation, payment completion). **All** admin-originated writes also write an audit log entry.

### 6.1 `adminGrantSubscription(uid, planId, durationDays, adminEmail?)`

Creates or replaces `users/{uid}/subscription/current` with a fresh subscription:

```ts
{
  planId,
  plan: planId,           // always duplicated
  status: 'active',
  startDate: Timestamp.now(),
  endDate: Timestamp.fromDate(now + durationDays),
  graceEndDate: Timestamp.fromDate(endDate + gracePeriodDays),
  trialUsed: false,
  autoRenew: false,
  paymentId: null,        // no payment — admin grant
  source: 'admin',
  createdAt: Timestamp.now(),
  updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
}
```

Audit log `action`: `'grant'`

Audit `newState` also includes `adminEmail` for display in the Giveaway Log.

---

### 6.2 `adminChangePlan(uid, planId)`

Partial merge into `users/{uid}/subscription/current`:

```ts
{
  planId,
  plan: planId,
  status: 'active',
  source: 'admin',
  updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
}
```

Audit log `action`:
- `'upgrade'` — new plan is higher tier than previous
- `'downgrade'` — new plan is lower tier
- `'admin_override'` — same tier (or unknown)

---

### 6.3 `adminExtendSubscription(uid, days)`

Extends the existing `endDate` by `days`. Base date is `max(now, existing endDate)`:

```ts
{
  endDate: Timestamp.fromDate(baseDate + days),
  graceEndDate: Timestamp.fromDate(newEnd + gracePeriodDays),
  status: 'active',
  source: 'admin',
  updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
}
```

Audit log `action`: `'extend'`

---

### 6.4 `adminCancelSubscription(uid)`

Immediately expires the subscription:

```ts
{
  status: 'expired',
  planId: 'free',
  plan: 'free',
  autoRenew: false,
  source: 'admin',
  updatedAt: Timestamp.now(),
}
```

Audit log `action`: `'cancel'`

---

### 6.5 `adminResetTrial(uid, performedByUid)`

Resets `trialUsed` on the **user document** (not the subscription):

```ts
// users/{uid}  ← setDoc with merge
{ trialUsed: false }
```

Audit log action: `'admin_reset_trial'`
`previousState`: `{ trialUsed: true }`
`newState`: `{ trialUsed: false }`

---

### 6.6 Main-app equivalents to write yourself

| User action | What to write | `source` | `action` in audit log |
|---|---|---|---|
| User starts free trial | `subscription/current` full doc | `'system'` | `'trial_start'` (your choice) |
| User completes payment | `subscription/current` full doc | `'payment'` | `'payment'` (your choice) |
| System detects expiry | merge `{ status: 'expired' }` | `'system'` | `'expire'` (your choice) |
| System detects grace | merge `{ status: 'grace' }` | `'system'` | `'grace'` (your choice) |

Always write a matching `subscription_logs` entry. The admin panel audit page reads from this collection to show a full history.

---

## 7. Payment Record Discovery

The admin Payment History page discovers payment records using a **Firestore collection-group query**:

```ts
getDocs(collectionGroup(db, 'subscription'))
// Matches every document in any sub-collection named 'subscription'
// i.e. users/*/subscription/current
```

A record appears in the payment history **only if** it has a non-null `paymentId`.

```ts
// Derives amount from the plan price
const price = planMap[data.planId]?.price ?? 0;
const amount = data.introOffer ? 0 : price;
```

This means:
- If `introOffer: true` → displayed amount is ₹0, even if plan has a price.
- If `paymentId: null` → record is excluded from payment history (e.g. admin grants, trials).

**Collectiongroup index requirement:** You must enable the `subscription` collection-group index in Firebase console for the query `getDocs(collectionGroup(db, 'subscription'))` to work without ordering. If you add `orderBy` you'll need a composite index.

---

## 8. Giveaway / Grant Log

The Giveaway Log page queries `subscription_logs` filtered to only `action === 'grant'`:

```ts
query(
  collection(db, 'subscription_logs'),
  where('action', '==', 'grant'),
  orderBy('timestamp', 'desc'),
)
```

Fields it reads from each log entry:
- `userId` — the affected user
- `newState.planId` or `newState.plan` — plan that was granted
- `newState.startDate` / `newState.endDate` — to compute duration
- `newState.adminEmail` or `data.adminEmail` — who performed the grant
- `timestamp` — when it happened

This means: when you write an admin grant audit log, the `newState` object **must** include `adminEmail` if you want it to appear correctly in the Giveaway Log.

---

## 9. Firestore Security Model

The admin panel comments document the intended rules:

```
isSuperAdmin() → request.auth.token.superAdmin === true
```

All admin write paths are gated behind this function. The main app user never has `superAdmin: true`.

**Expected rules structure (inferred):**

```
// Users can read/write their own documents
match /users/{uid} {
  allow read, write: if request.auth.uid == uid;

  match /subscription/current {
    allow read: if request.auth.uid == uid;
    allow write: if request.auth.uid == uid
                 || request.auth.token.superAdmin == true;
  }
}

// Admin-only collections
match /plans/{planId} {
  allow read: if request.auth != null;          // all authenticated users can read plans
  allow write: if request.auth.token.superAdmin == true;
}

match /config/{docId} {
  allow read: if request.auth != null;
  allow write: if request.auth.token.superAdmin == true;
}

match /announcements/{annoId} {
  allow read: if request.auth != null;
  allow write: if request.auth.token.superAdmin == true;
}

match /subscription_logs/{logId} {
  allow read: if request.auth.token.superAdmin == true;
  allow write: if request.auth != null;          // main app also writes logs
}

match /admins/{uid} {
  // NO client read — admin panel never reads this from client
  allow write: if request.auth.token.superAdmin == true;
}
```

> **Note:** The actual Firestore rules are deployed separately. The above is the intended model derived from the admin panel's auth strategy and usage patterns. Confirm with the actual rules file before deploying the main app.

---

## 10. Audit Log Reference

All possible `action` values written by the admin panel to `subscription_logs`:

| `action` value | Written by | Trigger |
|---|---|---|
| `'grant'` | `adminGrantSubscription` | Admin manually gives a free subscription |
| `'upgrade'` | `adminChangePlan` | Admin changes plan to a higher tier |
| `'downgrade'` | `adminChangePlan` | Admin changes plan to a lower tier |
| `'admin_override'` | `adminChangePlan` or `adminUpdateUserSubscription` | Admin changes to same tier or partial field update |
| `'extend'` | `adminExtendSubscription` | Admin adds days to existing subscription |
| `'cancel'` | `adminCancelSubscription` | Admin forces expiry and downgrades to free |
| `'admin_reset_trial'` | `adminResetTrial` | Admin resets `trialUsed` flag on user doc |

**Reserve these action values for the main app** (not currently used by admin panel, add your own as needed):

| Suggested `action` | Trigger |
|---|---|
| `'trial_start'` | User activates free trial |
| `'payment_success'` | User completes payment via Razorpay |
| `'auto_expire'` | System detects subscription past grace period |
| `'auto_grace'` | System detects subscription past end date |
| `'renewal'` | Razorpay auto-renew webhook succeeds |
| `'renewal_failed'` | Razorpay auto-renew webhook fails |

---

## 11. Key Business Rules

These rules are enforced by the admin panel and must be mirrored in the main app:

### 11.1 Grace period is always computed from `config/global`

```ts
const configSnap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'config', 'global'));
const gracePeriodDays = configSnap.data()?.gracePeriodDays ?? 3;  // default: 3
```

When writing a new subscription, always compute and store `graceEndDate`:

```ts
const graceEnd = new Date(endDate);
graceEnd.setDate(graceEnd.getDate() + gracePeriodDays);
```

### 11.2 Both `planId` and `plan` must always be written together

```ts
// Always write both:
{ planId: 'pro', plan: 'pro', ... }
// Never write only one.
```

### 11.3 `trialUsed` is on the user document, not the subscription

When a trial starts:
1. Write `subscription/current` with `status: 'trial'`, `source: 'system'`.
2. Merge `{ trialUsed: true }` into `users/{uid}`.
3. Check `users/{uid}.trialUsed` before offering a trial — if `true`, don't offer again even if the subscription record is gone.

### 11.4 Admin grants always have `paymentId: null`

Admin-granted subscriptions never appear in Payment History (which filters `paymentId != null`), but they do appear in the Giveaway Log (which filters `action == 'grant'`).

### 11.5 Intro offer pricing

If a user subscribes at ₹0 (introductory offer):
- Set `introOffer: true` on the subscription record.
- The Payment History page renders the amount as ₹0 when `introOffer === true`, regardless of plan price.

### 11.6 `source` field semantics

| `source` | When to use |
|---|---|
| `'system'` | Automated action — trial start, expiry detection, renewal webhook |
| `'admin'` | A human super-admin performed the action via the admin panel |
| `'payment'` | User completed a payment through Razorpay or another payment method |

### 11.7 UPI entries — filter by `isActive`

When displaying UPI payment options to users:

```ts
const activeUpiEntries = paymentConfig.upi.entries.filter(e => e.isActive);
```

### 11.8 Default grace period fallback

If `config/global` cannot be read (network error, rules), use `3` as the default `gracePeriodDays`. This is the hardcoded fallback in `adminGrantSubscription` and `adminExtendSubscription`.

### 11.9 `collectionGroup('subscription')` index

The admin Payment History page relies on a collection-group query on `subscription`. You must create a Firestore composite index in the Firebase console:

- **Collection group:** `subscription`
- **Fields indexed:** `paymentId` (Ascending), `updatedAt` (Descending) — or at minimum ensure collection-group queries are enabled.

### 11.10 Announcement expiry is client-side

The admin panel stores `expiresAt` as a Timestamp but does **not** use a Firestore `where('expiresAt', '>', now)` filter (which would require a composite index). Instead it fetches all active announcements and filters client-side. The main app should do the same to avoid index requirements:

```ts
const q = query(
  collection(db, 'announcements'),
  where('isActive', '==', true),
  orderBy('createdAt', 'desc')
);
const snaps = await getDocs(q);
const visible = snaps.docs
  .map(d => ({ id: d.id, ...d.data() }))
  .filter(a => {
    if (a.expiresAt && a.expiresAt.toDate() < new Date()) return false;
    // audience filtering...
    return true;
  });
```

You are adding a "Reset Trial" feature to the existing Users tab / User Management
section of the admin panel. A super admin should be able to reset the trialUsed
flag for any user so that user can receive a free trial again (support use case).

WHAT TO BUILD
-------------

   - Log the error to the console with prefix [AdminPanel][resetTrial].

- Do not touch users/{uid}/subscription/current.

Add a "Subscription Health" section to the existing admin dashboard home page.

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
FILE: attached_assets\Pasted-rules-version-2--1777755130159_1777755130160.txt
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
rules_version = '2';

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// Shopkeeper — Firestore Security Rules
// Project: shopkeeper-1a3fc
//
// ADMIN PANEL SETUP (one-time):
//   The Super Admin Panel must set a custom claim on each admin account:
//     admin.auth().setCustomUserClaims(uid, { superAdmin: true })
//   Until that is done, write access to config/plans/announcements is
//   blocked for everyone from the client (which is safe — seed data is
//   written during development via the Firebase Console or Admin SDK).
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service cloud.firestore {
  match /databases/{database}/documents {

    // ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    function isAuth() {
      return request.auth != null;
    }

    function isOwner(uid) {
      return isAuth() && request.auth.uid == uid;
    }

    // Super Admin Panel users carry a custom claim set by Firebase Admin SDK.
    function isSuperAdmin() {
      return isAuth() && request.auth.token.get('superAdmin', false) == true;
    }

    // Staff who have been granted access to a firm's namespace.
    // firm_accesses documents have fields: { user_id, firmUid, role }
    // We look up by a stable composite doc ID: "{staffUid}_{adminUid}"
    function hasStaffAccess(adminUid) {
      return isAuth() &&
        exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/firm_accesses/$(request.auth.uid + '_' + adminUid));
    }

    // ── User profile + all sub-collections ────────────────────────────────────

    match /users/{uid} {
      // Profile doc: owner or super admin
      allow read:   if isOwner(uid) || isSuperAdmin();
      // Writes include updating trialUsed, profile fields, etc.
      allow write:  if isOwner(uid) || isSuperAdmin();
    }

    // Subscription sub-document — owner reads/writes; super admin can override.
    match /users/{uid}/subscription/{doc} {
      allow read:   if isOwner(uid) || isSuperAdmin();
      allow write:  if isOwner(uid) || isSuperAdmin();
    }

    // Business data (transactions, parties, expenses, products, vehicles, waste,
    // ledger_entries, recycle_bin, settings, backup_meta, audit_logs, feedback,
    // error_logs, daily_snapshots, …)
    // Owner + staff with firm access + super admin.
    match /users/{uid}/{subcollection}/{docId} {
      allow read:  if isOwner(uid) || isSuperAdmin() || hasStaffAccess(uid);
      allow write: if isOwner(uid) || isSuperAdmin() || hasStaffAccess(uid);
    }

    // ── Subscription audit log ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    // Immutable from the client — create only. No updates or deletes.
    // A user can read their own entries; super admin can read all.

    match /subscription_logs/{logId} {
      allow create: if isAuth();
      allow read:   if isSuperAdmin()
                    || (isAuth() && resource.data.userId == request.auth.uid);
      allow update, delete: if false;
    }

    // ── Global config (config/global, config/payment_methods) ─────────────────
    // All authenticated users must be able to read:
    //   • config/global       — grace period, appMode, trial settings
    //   • config/payment_methods — UPI/bank details shown in SubscriptionTab
    // Only super admin can write.

    match /config/{doc} {
      allow read:  if isAuth();
      allow write: if isSuperAdmin();
    }

    // ── Subscription plans ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    // Authenticated users read plan details for SubscriptionTab display.
    // Only super admin can write.

    match /plans/{planId} {
      allow read:  if isAuth();
      allow write: if isSuperAdmin();
    }

    // ── Announcements ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    // AnnouncementBanner uses onSnapshot — all authenticated users must read.
    // Only super admin can create/update/delete.

    match /announcements/{announcementId} {
      allow read:  if isAuth();
      allow write: if isSuperAdmin();
    }

    // ── Multi-firm: firm accesses ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    // Document ID format: "{staffUid}_{adminUid}"
    // Admin (firmUid) creates records for their staff.
    // Staff can read their own access records.

    match /firm_accesses/{accessId} {
      allow read:   if isAuth() && (
                      resource.data.user_id  == request.auth.uid ||
                      resource.data.firmUid  == request.auth.uid ||
                      isSuperAdmin()
                    );
      allow create: if isAuth() && request.resource.data.firmUid == request.auth.uid;
      allow update: if isAuth() && resource.data.firmUid == request.auth.uid;
      allow delete: if isAuth() && (
                      resource.data.firmUid  == request.auth.uid ||
                      resource.data.user_id  == request.auth.uid
                    );
    }

    // ── Multi-firm: invitations ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    // Any authenticated user can read invitations (they need the code to accept).
    // Only the inviting admin can delete their own invitations.

    match /invitations/{invitationId} {
      allow read:   if isAuth();
      allow create: if isAuth();
      allow update: if isAuth() && (
                      resource.data.adminUid      == request.auth.uid ||
                      resource.data.invitedEmail  == request.auth.token.email
                    );
      allow delete: if isAuth() && resource.data.adminUid == request.auth.uid;
    }

    // ── User roles (in-app role assignments within a firm) ─────────────────────

    match /user_roles/{uid} {
      allow read:  if isOwner(uid) || isSuperAdmin();
      allow write: if isOwner(uid) || isSuperAdmin();
    }

  }
}

[END: attached_assets\Pasted-rules-version-2--1777755130159_1777755130160.txt]

const firebaseConfig = {

  authDomain: "shopkeeper-1a3fc.firebaseapp.com",

export const app  = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
export const auth = getAuth(app);
export const db   = getFirestore(app);

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
AUTHENTICATION — strict admin-only login
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
- Login with Firebase email/password only (no Google, no magic link)
- After login, immediately check Firestore: doc(db, 'admins', user.uid)
- If that doc does NOT exist → sign the user out immediately and show:
  "Access denied. You are not authorised to use this panel."
- If that doc EXISTS → allow access
- The admins/{uid} doc schema: { email: string, role: 'super_admin' | 'support', createdAt: Timestamp }
- Wrap the entire app in an AuthGuard component that redirects to /login
  if not authenticated
- On first load, show a full-screen loading spinner while auth state resolves
- Never expose any admin route to unauthenticated users

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FIRESTORE SCHEMA — these collections already exist in production
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

1. users/{uid}/subscription/current
   Fields:
     planId:       string          // 'free' | 'pro' | 'enterprise'
     plan:         string          // same as planId (legacy compat field)
     status:       'active' | 'trial' | 'expired' | 'grace'
     startDate:    Timestamp
     endDate:      Timestamp
     graceEndDate: Timestamp       // endDate + gracePeriodDays
     trialUsed:    boolean
     autoRenew:    boolean
     paymentId:    string | null
     source:       'system' | 'admin' | 'payment'
     introOffer:   boolean         // true = ₹0 launch promo user
     createdAt:    Timestamp
     updatedAt:    Timestamp

2. plans/{planId}  — planId is 'free', 'pro', or 'enterprise'
   Fields:
     name:         string
     price:        number          // in INR
     currency:     'INR'
     durationDays: number
     features:     string[]        // array of FeatureKey strings (see below)
     isActive:     boolean
     createdAt:    Timestamp
     updatedAt:    Timestamp

3. config/global   — single document
   Fields:
     freeTrialEnabled:  boolean
     trialDurationDays: number
     defaultPlan:       string     // 'free' | 'pro' | 'enterprise'
     gracePeriodDays:   number
     appMode:           'free' | 'paid' | 'hybrid'

4. subscription_logs/{autoId}   — immutable audit trail, never delete
   Fields:
     userId:        string
     action:        'create' | 'upgrade' | 'downgrade' | 'extend' | 'cancel' | 'admin_override' | 'expiry'
     previousState: object | null
     newState:      object
     performedBy:   'system' | 'admin'
     timestamp:     Timestamp

5. admins/{uid}
   Fields:
     email:     string
     role:      'super_admin' | 'support'
     createdAt: Timestamp

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FEATURE KEYS — exact strings used in plans[].features
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

'basic'              → "Core Billing"
'waste_tracking'     → "Waste Log"
'analytics'          → "Sales & Purchase Dashboards"
'advanced_analytics' → "Advanced Analytics"
'reports'            → "GST Reports"
'pos_billing'        → "POS Quick Billing"
'bulk_import'        → "Bulk CSV Import"
'stock_valuation'    → "Stock Valuation"
'game_timeline'      → "Activity Timeline"
'whatsapp_reminders' → "WhatsApp Reminders"
'multi_user'         → "Staff Accounts"

Free plan features:        ['basic', 'waste_tracking']
Pro plan features:         all 12 features above
Enterprise plan features:  all 12 features above

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
PAGES TO BUILD — React Router v6 routes
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Route: /login
  - Email + password form
  - On submit: signInWithEmailAndPassword → check admins/{uid} → allow or deny
  - Show inline error messages (wrong password, user not found, access denied)
  - No "Create account" link — admin accounts are created manually in Firestore

Route: / (dashboard, protected)
  - Summary cards:
      • Total users with active subscription
      • Total users on free plan
      • Total users on expired/grace subscription
      • Count of subscription changes in last 7 days (from subscription_logs)
  - Recent activity feed: last 20 entries from subscription_logs ordered by
    timestamp desc. Show: userId (truncated), action, performedBy, timestamp.
  - All counts loaded from Firestore on mount. Show skeleton loaders while loading.

Route: /users (protected)
  - Full user subscription list
  - Fetch: all docs from the users collection where a subscription/current
    sub-collection document exists. Use collectionGroup('subscription') to
    query all users at once.
  - Table columns: User ID (truncated, copyable), Plan, Status, End Date,
    Source, Intro Offer badge, Actions
  - Filter bar: filter by plan (all/free/pro/enterprise), status
    (all/active/expired/grace), search by user ID or email
  - Actions per row: "Change Plan", "Extend", "Cancel", "View Details"
  - Pagination: 25 users per page
  - Show a coloured status badge: active=green, trial=blue, expired=red,
    grace=orange
  - "Intro Offer" badge in yellow if introOffer === true

Route: /users/:uid (user detail, protected)
  - Full subscription record displayed in a card with all fields
  - Section: Subscription Actions
      • Change Plan: dropdown (free/pro/enterprise) + "Apply" button
      • Extend Subscription: number input (days) + "Extend" button
      • Cancel Subscription: red "Cancel" button with confirmation dialog
  - Section: Audit History
      • All subscription_logs where userId === uid, ordered by timestamp desc
      • Show action, performedBy, timestamp, previousState → newState diff

Route: /plans (protected)
  - List of all plans from plans/{planId}
  - Edit each plan inline: name, price, durationDays, isActive toggle, features checkboxes
  - "Save" button per plan — writes to Firestore using setDoc with merge:true
    and always sets updatedAt: Timestamp.now()
  - Feature checkboxes use the 12 feature keys above with their human labels
  - Visual indicator of which features are included vs excluded

Route: /config (protected)
  - Single form for config/global document
  - Fields: freeTrialEnabled (toggle), trialDurationDays (number),
    defaultPlan (dropdown), gracePeriodDays (number), appMode (radio)
  - "Save Config" button — writes to Firestore using setDoc with merge:true
  - Show last updatedAt if present in the doc

Route: /audit (protected)
  - Full audit log browser
  - Fetch all subscription_logs ordered by timestamp desc
  - Columns: User ID (copyable), Action, Performed By, Timestamp, Details
  - Click a row to expand: show previousState and newState as formatted JSON
  - Filter by action type and performedBy
  - Pagination: 50 rows per page

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
SERVICE LAYER — src/services/adminService.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
All Firestore writes go through this service. Never write to Firestore
directly in a component. Every mutation writes an audit log entry.

Implement these exact functions:

adminChangePlan(uid: string, planId: string): Promise<void>
  - Read current subscription → compute action (upgrade/downgrade)
  - Write: planId, plan, status:'active', source:'admin', updatedAt
  - Write audit log: action='upgrade'|'downgrade', performedBy='admin'

adminExtendSubscription(uid: string, days: number): Promise<void>
  - Read current endDate → extend by days from max(endDate, today)
  - Recompute graceEndDate = newEndDate + gracePeriodDays (read from config/global)
  - Write: endDate, graceEndDate, status:'active', source:'admin', updatedAt
  - Write audit log: action='extend', performedBy='admin'

adminCancelSubscription(uid: string): Promise<void>
  - Write: status:'expired', planId:'free', plan:'free', autoRenew:false,
    source:'admin', updatedAt
  - Write audit log: action='cancel', performedBy='admin'

adminUpdateUserSubscription(uid: string, payload: Partial<SubscriptionRecord>): Promise<void>
  - Generic override. Adds source:'admin', updatedAt.
  - Write audit log: action='admin_override', performedBy='admin'

writeAuditLog(entry): Promise<void>
  - addDoc to subscription_logs collection
  - Always include timestamp: Timestamp.now()
  - Serialize previousState/newState through JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(...))
    to strip undefined and non-serialisable values

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
LAYOUT & DESIGN — strict requirements
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
- Dark theme only. Background: #0f172a (slate-900). Cards: #1e293b (slate-800).
  Borders: #334155 (slate-700). Text: white / slate-400 for muted.
- Accent colour: indigo (#6366f1) for primary buttons and active nav items.
- Sidebar navigation (fixed left, 240px wide) with logo "Shopkeeper Admin"
  at top and nav links: Dashboard, Users, Plans, Config, Audit Log.
- Top bar showing logged-in admin email and a "Sign Out" button.
- All tables: alternating row backgrounds, hover highlight, sticky header.
- All destructive actions (Cancel subscription) require a confirmation modal
  with the text: "This will immediately expire the user's subscription.
  This cannot be undone. Type CONFIRM to proceed." and an input that must
  equal "CONFIRM" before the button enables.
- All buttons show a loading spinner while their async action is in progress.
- Toast notifications for every action: success (green) or error (red).
  Auto-dismiss after 4 seconds. Stack up to 3 toasts.
- Skeleton loaders (grey pulsing blocks) for every data table while loading.
- Responsive: sidebar collapses to top nav on screens < 768px.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE STRUCTURE — follow this exactly
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

    firebase.ts          ← exact config from above

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
TYPES — define all of these in src/types/index.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

export interface SubscriptionRecord {
  planId: string;
  plan: string;
  status: 'active' | 'trial' | 'expired' | 'grace';
  startDate: any;        // Firestore Timestamp
  endDate: any;          // Firestore Timestamp
  graceEndDate: any;     // Firestore Timestamp
  trialUsed: boolean;
  autoRenew: boolean;
  paymentId: string | null;
  source: 'system' | 'admin' | 'payment';
  introOffer?: boolean;
  createdAt: any;
  updatedAt: any;
}

export interface UserWithSubscription {
  uid: string;
  subscription: SubscriptionRecord;
}

export interface Plan {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  price: number;
  currency: 'INR';
  durationDays: number;
  features: string[];
  isActive: boolean;
  createdAt: any;
  updatedAt: any;
}

export interface GlobalConfig {
  freeTrialEnabled: boolean;
  trialDurationDays: number;
  defaultPlan: string;
  gracePeriodDays: number;
  appMode: 'free' | 'paid' | 'hybrid';
}

export interface AuditLog {
  id: string;
  userId: string;
  action: string;
  previousState: Record<string, any> | null;
  newState: Record<string, any>;
  performedBy: 'system' | 'admin';
  timestamp: any;
}

export interface AdminUser {
  uid: string;
  email: string;
  role: 'super_admin' | 'support';
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
CRITICAL RULES — never break these
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Never write directly to Firestore in a component — always call adminService.ts
2. Every Firestore write must produce an audit log entry (subscription_logs)
3. Every admin action must write source:'admin' and updatedAt:Timestamp.now()
4. When extending a subscription, always recompute graceEndDate
5. When changing a plan, always write BOTH planId AND plan fields (backward compat)
6. Destructive actions (cancel) require the CONFIRM modal — no exceptions
7. Never delete from subscription_logs — it is an immutable audit trail
8. Timestamps: use Timestamp.now() from 'firebase/firestore' for all writes.
   For display, convert using .toDate() then format with date-fns format()
9. Use collectionGroup('subscription') to query all user subscriptions in
   one call rather than reading every user doc individually
10. All async operations must show loading state and handle errors with toast

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
WHAT TO BUILD FIRST (do it in this order)
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
1. Install all dependencies
2. src/config/firebase.ts
3. src/types/index.ts
4. src/services/adminService.ts
5. src/context/AuthContext.tsx
6. src/components/Layout.tsx, AuthGuard.tsx, ConfirmModal.tsx,
   Toast.tsx, SkeletonTable.tsx, StatusBadge.tsx

15. Verify the app builds with zero TypeScript errors (run tsc --noEmit)
16. Take a screenshot and confirm the login page loads correctly

Do not stop after any step — complete the entire build before returning.
If TypeScript gives errors, fix them before moving on.
Do not ask the user any clarifying questions — everything you need is above.

You are updating the Admin Panel (React + Firebase) to become the **single authority for subscription control**.

The app NO LONGER auto-grants any subscription.
All access must be controlled by **backend payments or admin actions only**.

---

# 🧠 SYSTEM CONTEXT

There are 3 systems:

* App → reads subscription
* Backend → writes subscription on payment
* Admin Panel → manually controls subscription

👉 You are responsible for **manual control only**

---

# 🚨 NON-NEGOTIABLE RULES

❌ Do NOT auto-create subscriptions
❌ Do NOT assume any user has Pro
❌ Do NOT change schema
❌ Do NOT write partial data

✅ Always write full subscription object
✅ Always log audit actions
✅ Always keep schema consistent

---

# 📦 FIRESTORE STRUCTURE (STRICT)

---

## Subscription document

```ts id="4xq4sb"
users/{uid}/subscription/current
```

---

## Required fields

```ts id="n4j6ya"
{
  planId: string,
  plan: string,
  status: 'active' | 'trial' | 'grace' | 'expired',
  startDate: timestamp,
  endDate: timestamp,
  graceEndDate: timestamp,
  paymentId: string | null,
  source: 'admin' | 'payment' | 'system',
  autoRenew: boolean,
  updatedAt: timestamp
}
```

---

## Audit logs

```ts id="xy5k8f"
subscription_logs/{autoId}
```

---

## Audit log format

```ts id="1df9y3"
{
  userId,
  action,
  previousState,
  newState,
  performedBy: 'admin',
  timestamp
}
```

---

# 🔧 ADMIN ACTIONS (IMPLEMENT ALL)

---

## 1. Grant Subscription

* Select plan
* Set:

```ts id="1xhv5m"
status = 'active'
source = 'admin'
paymentId = null
```

* Compute:

  * startDate = now
  * endDate = now + durationDays

---

## 2. Upgrade Plan

* Replace planId
* Extend from:

```ts id="zqk0qk"
baseDate = max(now, existing.endDate)
```

---

## 3. Downgrade to Free

```ts id="r7hnh9"
planId = 'free'
status = 'active'
```

---

## 4. Extend Subscription

* Add X days to endDate

---

## 5. Cancel Subscription

```ts id="j9lp88"
status = 'expired'
```

---

## 6. Override Subscription (Admin Fix)

* Allow full manual editing
* Must still respect schema

---

## 7. Reset Trial

```ts id="d1avc6"
users/{uid}.trialUsed = false
```

---

# 🔁 IMPORTANT LOG ACTIONS

Use EXACT values:

```ts id="uxv08k"
admin_grant
admin_upgrade
admin_downgrade
admin_extend
admin_cancel
admin_override
admin_reset_trial
```

---

# 🧩 UI REQUIREMENTS

For each user show:

* current plan
* status
* expiry
* source
* paymentId (if exists)

---

## Add controls:

* dropdown → select plan
* buttons → grant / extend / cancel / downgrade

---

# 🔄 REAL-TIME SYNC

Use:

```ts id="ytb7y6"
onSnapshot()
```

👉 Admin sees updates instantly

---

# ⚠️ EDGE CASES

---

## Case 1 — No subscription doc

👉 Treat as Free
👉 Do NOT write automatically

---

## Case 2 — Existing subscription

👉 Always preserve previousState for logs

---

## Case 3 — Expired subscription

👉 Allow extend or upgrade

---

# ❌ DO NOT

❌ Do NOT call payment APIs
❌ Do NOT handle Razorpay
❌ Do NOT store secrets

---

# 🧪 TEST CASES

---

### Test 1

Admin grant → app unlocks instantly

### Test 2

Admin cancel → app locks

### Test 3

Admin extend → expiry updates

### Test 4

Logs correctly recorded

---

# ✅ EXPECTED RESULT

* Admin fully controls subscription
* No auto behavior in app
* Clean audit logs
* System consistent across app + backend

---

Focus on strict schema adherence and full control.
